Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For he finds a bite also as from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the bite has passed, lift your hand with the tool and raise the buttock gently, and leave it like this for three days, and put on butter until what is black from the scorching is whitened;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	And let it be for three days as decay sets in;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be the final aid after the treatment of ointments until it is sound.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended to the thigh or to the leg, you apply the same tool that marks the buttocks according to what you did on the hip equally.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is how one handles the hot application, and I have written it out as part of my treatise on correcting medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take quicklime and fresh chalk in equal parts, grind them together, and put the mixture into a new jar.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	If there is a small opening so that the tip of a razor may enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	And place another pot well filled with water, and put it on an oven and some heat sources under it, until there are two layers of powders above your hand when you have properly taken it in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	And let it stay like this until all the essence, dung or grease has drained out or water boils, then take all that essence, and pour it onto heat sources such as charcoal and alkali in the same manner before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will become water and be administered in the form of preparations for medicine and in cauterizations for other parts of the body.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it achieves the same effect as fire, and is used with other medicines such as when cauterizing well in the hip like turpentine and almond oil with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a remedy that was used for the pain in the hip and sciatic vein, and to a great extent. He says that no other treatment was done, and it worked miraculously on its first use when this cure was applied, and he took baths as is instructed below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And instructs in this manner that you take dry and fresh verdigris, and grind it finely with a little fat, and spread it on the hip and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain resides, and bind it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And leave it for three hours, ensuring that the patient does not feel any burning from the remedy.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make them enter into a warm bath until their body is slightly revived, and make them rest on a bed, and the pain will leave them completely and they will feel well.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicines as the cautery, unless after the removal of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides states that when the sciatic vein is treated with donkey's milk, it helps a lot;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And the application of the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take wool and soak it in old oil, and place it on the depression that is between the first toe of the foot and the other one called the foscile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After obtaining dry donkey's milk, apply it over the fire until it becomes charcoal, and place it on the cloth, leaving it until it turns black;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And repeat this again, and never stop doing so until you think by sense it will come up to the waist, and that the pain should cease.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And this method of cautery is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by falling or impact or from too much evacuation, or due to exposure to cold matter, none of these conditions warrant cauterization, for it is akin to what arises from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	After which, when the body is void of fetid pills or other similar things, one should apply them on the back, where the pain resides, three lines marked in a cross pattern, and in each line perform V cauterizations or more according to the virtue and quantity that the body can endure;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And let the cauterizations be done according to the cautery which is called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	And if you see fit, perform three or four cauterizations halfway along the median line of the cautery in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This illness often befalls young children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have pale cheeks when they sit up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find in the last spinal vertebra of the back and within us the appearance that comes over the other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe its cure, if you apply it with a hot iron in this manner on the body.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cautery burns each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see it, apply the cautery to the spine along the line where the cauterization burns for two or three lines, and have the points close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the cure as long as it is clean according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply the cautery in a state of excitement near nerves.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain in joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain is due to moist substances that spread throughout each limb of the body, and when pain comes into bones, which they call "gout" properly, and when it's caused by cold and cannot be cured by medicines alone, if it needs treatment with cauteries in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the mouth of the cautery inside the joint of the foot, and apply the olive oil cautery according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need that you touch on the thigh by the foot, if it is cauterized with the entire cautery saying 'point'.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains extend up to the knees and other joints, which happens many times, have it apply the cautery on each knee three or four of each part, for all the olive oil cautery;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need to do more, do it more, but don't keep your hand out of the way until the wound is well healed.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend as far as the thighs and back, then it is administered to them the cautery that we have said in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, make points inside the wrist region;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there remains any pain in the arms, make points on each joint and on the back of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains come up to the elbows or to the shoulders, cauterize each part, and give good care to the patient and administer remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	And if you give them good governance and cleanse the humor, they will be helped by God to recover their health.
de la routure dou syfac	from the rupture of the uterus
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When an injury affects the lungs and the bowels descend into the womb, if this is a new occurrence, it's important that when you see the wounds being treated, you do not eat on that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	And when one consumes things which relax the stomach, so that his innards descend from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After you have made them sit on their back between your hands, and instruct them to shave their armpits until the hair is neatly trimmed, and remove it with your fingers, and pay attention to feeling under the cut at the bone, and at all times make sure it appears as half a circle above the chest;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat up the cautery tool described here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it is white and emits serents.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then remove the bowels to their proper place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and have the assistants shave his hands so they don't twist around backwards;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	work well on the thighs with the patient, and place a servant and a sergeant by his legs, and another at his feet who will shave his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery at the mark on your hand, and hold it straight until you touch the bone, and if you do not touch it in the first try, keep trying again as long as you reach to the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and know that the boil should not overflow when you apply the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so as to not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so that the patient does not die or suffer any other harm from this treatment.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not come all the way to the bone with the cautery, your operations are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterizations for children be subtle according to their size, and also large enough for adults according to theirs.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, apply the butter cautery until the scab is removed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After the treatment with other ointments until it is healed, and let the patient lie on his back for forty days so that the wound heals well.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that these remedies be given for a long time so that the urine does not overflow when they want to go to the chamber.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, if he wants to stand up, have him supported by a well-made belt, and wear it for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And have him get proper rest, so that he doesn't overwork himself and avoids too much drinking and eating, as well as shouting too loudly.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when he follows this instruction, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say after this chapter's treatment of tailoring.
de la routure dou ventre	regarding the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ulcers occur in other bellies and are noticeable, and you see that they no longer grow, then treat them with a fire cautery according to their quantity, and heat it three parts of the pot.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	Following the treatment as we have explained;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And none of the old ones said that one should be cauterized with a three-cornered cautery according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	The first sign is the beginning of healing; draw a line across the width above the wound and another below it, and hold your hand with the fire tool all along.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	The first cauterizations are lighter and heal more easily.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in no limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether from falling or being hit, and the pain lasts for a long time, and medicine cure doesn't help it, then it should be cauterized with what is called "points" cautery, and the cauterizations must match the length of the member and its smallness and weakness and its function and location of twisting and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it responds well to the first cautery, that's good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If it bears this name, start another cautery on that spot, for such injuries typically require the affected limb to respond, so you must perform the cauteries until the patient shows improvement.
de meselerie	Regarding cautery from fire, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The healings take place once every cautery with considerable assistance, and similarly the disease comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can't you see her being cauterized? Take care that the disease is in its beginning stages, and if it's treated according to what we've said in this section, without getting worse or staying stagnant, and you're unsure whether the infection will spread throughout the body, then perform five cauterizations on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I lead the head towards nine, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hair.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and above the two horns, and one behind on the back.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and hold your hand so that the cautery reaches up to the bone, and until the scabs come out sufficiently that the fumes of the large humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the mouse according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the mixture spreads everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	And if it becomes clear that it is lost, then you should cauterize with these cauteries as we have described: on the head with one, and over the nose with another, and two over the spine of the neck, and six over the spine of the back, and one large on the ribcage and another beneath it, and two over the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	And on the cuts, and on the tendons at the heel, and once on each joint of hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	And beware of the nerves that are behind the heel, do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And never apply a cautery to the bone of the thumb, and once on the bone of the stomach, and once on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more I apply the cautery, the more aid I give, and it benefits him;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the sick do not feel pain from the cautery as the healthy would, for their body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterizing fires be large and small according to the limbs and joints, as you will find in the methods of metalworking.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the treatment, use flour mixed with honey and other treatments until it becomes healthy again.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medications, oils, and bandages, but it remains uncured, then I will apply cauterizations to the limb according to its size and dimensions;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let the cauterizations touch slightly within the thigh's depth;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply the ointment cure until it becomes healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And then perform cauterization to the arm and foot and back, at the end of the nerve that makes the limb move, and thus it is healed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And yet, no one should interfere unless they are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	Of cauteries, instruct the patient to let their hair grow long and evenly; if they prick at their roots when young, hold them steady so they don't move until grown out.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" has progressed and medicine treatment is ineffective, then apply a small cauterization using a cautery, according to the depth of the thigh, until the boil is drained and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then mix with flour of almonds and lentils and rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood of colostrum and blood of quail, from each a part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And mix everything together, and bind it with a cloth, and expose it to the air until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of a sore by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When gangrene begins, and you see it start to halt, if you notice it at the outset, apply a cautery instrument that appears like a circle, all around the circumference of the gangrene.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And still, some surgeons advised that one should apply the cautery also in the middle of the ulcer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	And still, I don't think that's good either, for fear it might get infected and rot, and I've already decided not to do it that way ever again;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the more effective thing is to apply the cautery internally, with the one called "circular" cautery, as we have mentioned in terms of various types of cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness which is called "adubelati", and it prolongs death or because of the excess she does or due to age in the weakening of the malady when it becomes old (meaning too old) and they have little blood, or due to tension;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hastening towards death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	therefore, apply the cautery around with several small applications;
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterwards leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced through with all the cautery, heat the cautery as shown here:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this illness which is called "adubelati" as long as the fire points through its heart, and make such cauterizations that the patient feels it beyond in such a way that the course of corruption becomes easier.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure until it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The fire cure by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another form of illness exists which is called 'corrodens', and this is nothing else but a member affection, as it burns the limbs just like you would dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in them that can bear a complete fire cautery, then apply small and large iron cauterizing tools, according to what is suitable for the place or where the illness is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	Afterwards apply the cautery from all sides until you remove all the corruption, and leave nothing behind, making sure that every corrupted part is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And leave it for three days, and apply burning with oil on the burnt areas until the burned scabs have healed, and all the corruption has disappeared.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of ointments that generate pus.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days you see that a clean one does not emerge, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if not, then restart the application of the cautery on what remains stuck beneath the corrupted shoulder.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this method was once treated with herbal medicines instead of applying heat to the cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	However, the heat cautery is still greatly beneficial, and I have already explained the treatment with herbal medicines in this section.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take what you need when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the roots coming to stones
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Sometimes it happens that a disease arises through cracks in the skin which we call "cyst," according to our understanding, and it is a large lump that irritates the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterizations for this disease do so in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This means fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	The fire cautery should be prepared as if you were sharpening a piece of iron like a feather, and it should be made from good quality metal in such a way that it can accommodate nails in all directions, and it should have thin edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After setting everything on fire under the nail, and turn your hand fully around the nail until it reaches the tip of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave him like this for three days until signs of gangrene begin to appear;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make him a poultice of wild marjoram ground with vinegar, and leave the poultice overnight, and he will pull out his nails cleanly from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound by cleaning it thoroughly until it is clean.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they have turned outside the nails, and this happens many times in hands and feet, then you should bring them to a hot water cautery;
et est en teil maniere:	and is done like this:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take an arrow shaft or iron rod, or a feather from a goose, and place it on the nail and the thorn, that is to say, for warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the coal on it until it burns all around, then add a little warm ash, and keep your hand firmly. Squeeze your hand as you turn so that the edge of the coal reaches to the base of the nail, and then find the deep hot water source down to the base;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	And allow the patient to endure for a bit, the application of the hot water for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then leave it like this, and all its roots will be eradicated completely.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Start one after another, until you have treated all those inside the body, then treat the sores that produce pus.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment for shaking
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When there are tremors due to cold or nerves, or a quartan fever or any other ailment, it is necessary that you apply four fire cauteries or four on the spine of the back, one fire cautery between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	And for the fire cautery, place it on the stomach with an olive oil cautery.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If it causes trembling, and hasten the recovery of the cold illness's health.
des pustules puans	puant sores
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	When any sign of disease becomes visible through the skin, or pus-filled ulcers appear, these come from large decayed materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	It is necessary at the beginning when they appear that one makes a cautery on each head of the boil:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A fine firebrand from the wood of myrtle, whose points are taken by the flame, or from the long root of aristolochia, or with a lentiscus cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And each time they cauterize them at the beginning when they are visible, according to this method, and they cannot grow any pus further in front, but it discharges all the excess that causes them, and they become healthy;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	But it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery has been cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there were great flows of blood from the artery that is tied at the wound, which comes outwards, or during an incision near the abscess, or with the cautery on the member, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	And it's very unpleasant to stink.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet, when this happens to none of them, if you rush to place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and hold tightly until the pulse subsides under your finger, and no more drops come out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then place several small and large olive oil cauteries on fire until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then take me, large or small depending on the wound and its location where the artery runs, place the cautery near that vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cautery there until the pulse is completely stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you remove your finger from the vein, and the cauteries are extinguished, take quickly another one of the cauteries that are at the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And keep doing this one after another until the wound is healed;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and be sure not to burn the nerve that lies within, and let no other harm come upon the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	know that when you cut off the artery, one cannot properly set it without damage even if the artery is large; this can be managed through any of the four methods we have discussed:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cautery, or by extraction if it hasn't been treated yet, or by strong threading of the wound with a thread, or by medicines applied which have the power to heal blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and bind and restrain it properly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the reattachment, by tightly binding with cloths or placing hot things on, or other similar actions, if it doesn't benefit them.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they have no means or medicine at hand, should place their finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it well until it is healed above the wound and above the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	And it must not be moved; but it should be moistened with cold water often until it is very cold, as long as the ice remains frozen and thickened and stays put.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And prepare for those who need cauterization and medications.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of treatments for amputations
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases for which fire cautery or hot medicines are needed, and we discussed their uses, causes, instruments, and forms of application.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	And I have placed this chapter about the shoulder joint until the elbow, and I will proceed with this chapter in a similar manner for those who find it easier to understand these concepts.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And as I start this, it must be known that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first chapter of using the fire cauterizations, and for this reason, more caution is needed.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the treatment of this chapter, there are often blood evacuations when opening veins and making incisions on abscesses, as well as treatments for wounds, extraction of arrows, and incisions into stones, among other similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For there is doubt and fear, and many die as a result.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you that you do not engage in foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For none of the ways of people come to remedies.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	If they come from those who suffered so much with their illness that they died lightly due to the panic they found in their disease, and the severity of their suffering;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And out of this, one should have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And concerning these, I am given the sense to say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am afraid";
et li maladie est despitouse.	And the disease is malicious.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not right for you to consent to those who come to you in this manner. Instead, place more emphasis on your dignity than on your greed and do not rashly but wisely open up about what you are sure of and where you can take control;
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	And use prognosis and guidance in your treatments for ailments where health is converted.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you to gain good reputation, fame, and lasting memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear son, Our Lords give you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to inspire by the holy inspiration of their hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have instructed you this chapter by considering it in parts, according to what is before or the section about cauteries that I have discussed up until the foot, so you will find it easier to understand for those who need it.
dou chief plein d’aigue	the head filled with water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often comes from when the baby is born, and when the mother holds the baby's head too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And it never comes about due to any fault that we know of.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I never saw this disease occur except in children, and among all those whom I have seen, it hastened their deaths;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And because of this, it seems to me that I should divide the work into parts for treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw the child of whom the shoulder was full of water, and the head swelled each day to the point that it couldn't withstand it anymore;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	And he suffered so much from moisture that he died, and this moisture is assembled around the bone at the elbow, between the flesh and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	And the operations are like this: when moisture is between the flesh and bone, and the abscesses are small that you cut through with a large incision in the head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and as long as II thumbs, provided the moisture is contained.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and here is the shape of the sputum:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, then make two cuts in a cross-shaped manner, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is around the bone, and you see the signs that I'm talking about - when the corners of each part of the head are open, and when pressing it with your hand internally causes a sharp pain, and this does not respond to touch:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary for you to make three cuts within the head, following this method:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all moisture completely outside.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After holding the cuts with lint and powders, and I put wine and oil, then leave like this until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then release it, and treat the wound with bandages and dressings, and allow the head to heal evenly, and afterwards give the patient dry meat from a small animal while the limb is reinforced and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to look at where the opening of the abscess is large, and gather together the water;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	because it is not always in front;
aucune fois derrier;	nor always behind;
aucune fois en destre;	No once in the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and no once in the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	So cut or incise the wound open, and fill with water, and let the process follow according to your capability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful not to clip the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and observe for blood flow, so that the patient dies from the circulation of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	In reference to cautery using fire, command the patient to allow hair growth until it becomes long and uniform; if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they fully grow.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it comes to any illness that is called 'catarrh' in the eyes or at the bottom of the nose and such diseases are old, and the cure from medicine doesn't bring benefit, then the final treatment includes cauterization along with cutting off the two main arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	So, when you see them clip, make sure the patient has moved past their head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After rubbing the wound with a rough cloth until the arteries are visible, then pull the patient's head back with all the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein is placed, and the ears of each are after them, and the back is properly recovered;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the ears of each, then cut both with a sharp scalpel for two parts, until you see the vein up to the bone, and this must be done by cutting across the main artery.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it, pinch off the sperm on both sides of the artery and vein above, cut them also as two inches through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the veins are incised, let the blood flow out continuously from up high.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open upon being pressed, it is necessary to measure three digits of space there, then cut into the ear until you reach the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	And what needs to be removed of the blood is six cubic centimeters, and by chance either a little more or less, depending on how the patient can tolerate it, and the filling of the artery;

s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it stays at the spot where the spur touches, then cut off the abscess and if there's no residue, then clean the wound and bind it, and apply ointment treatment until it heals.

Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old age arrives, and severe coughing comes along, due to moisture from tears and heat in the temples and elsewhere throughout one's aging body, as well as similar things. The treatment is done through ways of medicine cure techniques and all such methods do not benefit it fully; we would extract the arteries in the temples and cauterize them, just like what we have recounted.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the way of their extraction is that the physician makes incisions behind the temples of his patient, and listens to the artery which appears in the temple, because it opens well through its beating, and is only responsive in some very cold men;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it responds, then hold the neck of some cloths under the artery, then rub its back with some rough cloth, and immerse its body in hot water until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Then take the spatula of which this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Then lightly remove the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it upwards with forceps, and carefully remove all the webs that are in between each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the artery is delicate, twist it with the tip of the hook, then cut that part according to the size of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it isn't cut, neither does it spring forth without pain completely.

puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut off the excess that is between the two threads at this moment. por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	because it is of greater assistance for drying.

And the one that is softer and more easily extracted in removing a vessel, you should apply this cautery to cut the vein with two parts, but make sure those cuts are well spaced to retain heat for longer periods.

des larmes	Of tears
