dou reume des eulz	from the pus of the bones
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When there's no usual cough coming from the lungs, and you see that the eyes are tired and small, and weaken sight, and burned papers;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	And the hair grows, and one feels fullness up to the bone with pain, and the patient coughs;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	Therefore, know through these events that this matter and this cathartic comes only from many veins, and the moist cure that is present, if it is such.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And you must instruct the patient to look behind their forehead, then create a large cut above the forehead, and another one somewhat below it.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And begin from the crease of the left temple to the right temple, and make the incision up to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move when eating;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	And when the bone is revealed, let all the blood drain onto a sponge, and then soak it between the two lips of the incision and place old cotton and linen;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then drape it with wet cloths in wine and oil, and beware of pus forming;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	When it is extracted, you should rub the bone until cartilage begins to grow, then treat with excising substances that encourage cartilage growth.
En teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts of the flower of wheat and four parts of the flower of comfrey, and make it into a paste;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and apply it to these wounds to encourage the growth of cartilage throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Regarding ear piercing
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Everything that drops in your ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	it could be grains, or an animal, or stone from earth, or anything similar like iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or seeds, such as beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or anything that flows out like water and oil and similar substances.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When it comes to piercing the ear or any other way of doing things that do not fit with the ear or does not grow in the ear, place the ear under the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see a stone, if it discharges any drop of purple oil or nut oil, then proceed with extraction;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and you make him sneeze with consin, and stop his nostrils when the sneezing comes on, and place pieces of cloth or wool inside the ear;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and keep the ear above.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Many times, strength comes through this cure;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come about, then one proceeds with the extraction using fine forceps, which is done in this manner:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it jumps out through the forceps, that's good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if not, then proceed with the extraction using a small slender scalpel;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	And if it doesn't leap from this, make an armpit needle and pinch the tip of the needle or the stem of the ear strongly, and immerse whatever is inside the candle wax so that the wick cannot enter with the needle;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	Then let the treatment continue, because many times it goes like what we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	And if it doesn't come forth in that manner, take some glue and mix with it its oils, and insert with each an instrument that suits for this task, and put a little cotton inside;
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	Then press the glue onto the stone or anything else, and continue with force.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it doesn't leap with all these things that we have said, then you must hasten to pierce the ear in such a way that pus and bad things may come out, and do so without delay.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	And the method of making the incision is that you first make the patient bleed from the cephalic vein and drain out blood according to its size, then place the patient under your hands and turn their head upwards, and create a small cut at the base of the ear where the fat hangs down.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	And make the incision as wide as a crescent moon until you reach the bone. Then remove the bone according to your ability and suck it quickly into your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat until the patient is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if it's grains that have formed and they're swollen, then perform an extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	And if it can't come out, then administer the thin paste below according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make an incision on that seed.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not do this when you think that the beans are wet due to ear moisture, until you have done many pieces of work;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	Then extract the delicate pinpricks and from the sweat gland, just like we said before, so that the extractions are smooth.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In water then, when a person vomits in the ear, it is required that the patient uses spitting of cold liquids first, and fully fills the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let it rest on the same ear or where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If she jumps for heaven, that's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, take many stones according to the length of your finger tips and gently, and warm them slightly on fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	And place the patient's ear in or slightly to the side of their own ear, and take another step away from it on one foot, and cut open with another stone inside the stone that is in the ear;
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	And do not stop changing stones from one to another until the heat comes out completely, and thus it will come out all its strength;
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	And if you see it, take hold of the branch, and push one end into the ear, and the other end with fire until the most tender part is charred;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then repeat this process for other branches, until the sharp tip comes out completely, as we have said about stones.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of a small beast, like a flea and similar things, treat it as we have said in the case of dissection;
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it's large and could be felt, undertake the extraction using forceps;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	And this is the easier thing to remove that is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worm-like things from the ears, when you have tried as we have said in dissection and with steam treatments, if the treatment is not beneficial, then you should observe the ear under sunlight:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If there are no gaps, then use fine needles to pierce, and if not seen, take the thread from which this shape is found:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And may be narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And apply the finest tip in the ear according to the amount of suffering from the patient's complaint, then fully shape all the vein;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Do this often until all the blood flows out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not flow out, then immerse the cotton thread in the vein as I said for cutting into the stone;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	And if they do not protrude as we have said, administer distillations that the old have proven effective in removing worms, and you will find guidance on distillations;
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	And if you apply your oils and medications to the ear using this tool, as depicted here for you to see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And whether it be made of silver or of a prickly weed, place it under the small openings and use it to distill;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	And to press inside the distillation with a well-made arnica tool for this purpose; and if you see that you are grasping and enveloping around the cotton appendage at the tip.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	Then pour your oil or juice, and what you see of your medicine in the cane, let the cane be inside the ear;
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	Then place all the cotton inside the grasp, and press your hand in rhythm until the oil is distilled or the ear has enough exposure;
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	And within it you feel the sensation of the patient, and if there is a distillation that is heated in the fire thus it's distilled into the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	And remember that it should not be too cold, because the medicine would not be as good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Regarding ear piercing
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born without any perforations in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	The same thing happens with adults due to wounds or birth in the ear of a fetus, and these injuries often enter the ear from behind, unless one can see them;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	And it never happens that the hole disappears from the perforation, and you will see this well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	That which comes from behind, if you cannot see it, is usually a sign of improper healing in various conditions. And it appears that you should place the ear near the patient's face towards the sun;
et regarde dedens:	And look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	and if you see the superficial pustule, if it is of this form from what has been mentioned:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And may they be equally deep in front and behind, without touching the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the pustule is of new flesh or part of the ear, use delicate pricking and gently scrape it, until that flesh is entirely removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the wicks go into the ear canal, take a fine, light wax and melt it with fire for a little bit, then put it inside the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the pustule that causes pain in the ear from the patient, prick gently, and make sure not to damage the nerves of the ear;
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	Then place in the ear a tent according to the width of the pustule, and smear with the Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Continue this treatment every day until the wound is healed. Or take an emetic and mix it with pink water, then powder the vitriol ground.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And if you see the ear swelling up, it's necessary to take the emetic and stir another wet emetic made of rose oil and beeswax, until the swelling is removed.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then continue to treat it as long as it remains sound.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, immerse an sponge and soak it in cold water, then place it on the ear, and perform other treatments that stop bleeding which include remedies for distillations.
de la char des papieres	From the substance of the papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	By the end of the month that comes written on the papers about the eyes when they are wet and dry, it's necessary to spread them with tongs and forceps, and use a poultice from its roots;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	Then place sulfur on the area of vitriol ground.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if it cannot be stripped off, then use a fine lens cautery to cauterize it, and the cauterizer should do so after making an incision.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	And many times they return, yet nothing remains of their roots;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	And when they are cauterized by fire, their roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	Regarding ice or cold treatments
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times come in papers some things that seem to have a crust by their shape and hardness, and for this reason it is called "hail disease", and it's an accumulation of moisture within the paper above and below.
li ovraiges est telz:	The work proceeds as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Take care that the hail does not move from one side to another, and it is a light matter to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Begin with a wide cut, then lightly sear each part of the body, afterwards grip it with forceps, and hold.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	if you can't hold it without piercing a bit of the paper, so long as you don't harm the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	and if it splits widely, then stitch it up with a seam, and treat until it's healed;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if it's small, do not exert much force, for the ointments will heal it quickly and nourish flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the stone descends into the ear towards the upper part, then turn it upside down, and get the stone to one of the forceps, hold it, press from both sides;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	And if paper is removed by incision, this causes no harm;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	And when the ice is removed, wash out the salt water and cleanse the wound as long as the patient's health improves.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the lumps
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a grease that accumulates on the sheets of papers above it, and this happens more often in children than adults, causing much trouble for their eyes. It causes them to urinate early in the morning, and they cannot look at the sun's light because tears rush to their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And because of this, they lie down in their own feces and sleep there, and have wet papers under their buttocks that smell like excrement and give them an appearance covered with the grease which opens in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press on your hand with your fingers and feel exinach between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the method of treatment is such that the patient puts their head back to its healthy position;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	and then take flax cloth, and set up a tent in manner of a circle according to the quantity that flows out from each part, then place it on them;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your thumbs on both sides, so that the discharge is collected within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then in the middle of the moisture at the skin, cut a slit diagonally, and make it neither too wide nor larger than the wound we do for vein opening surgery;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and stretch the skin around until you see the discharge;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and in various positions, discharge comes out of the slit, resembling a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Pull out then take one whole strip of surgical cloth between your fingers at the front end, and turn your hand to the right and left until it is spread out;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	and make sure not to adjust in the cut, that you do not bleed all the way up to the eye, that you do not blister it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the cut does not open at the beginning of the cut, so enlarge a bit gently the cut until it opens;
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	then pull it as we have said, then moisten with water and vinegar and place on the wound, and bind with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And if there are such people who grind salt and put it on to corrupt that moisture which has remained.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the treatment should continue as long as it is effective.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to the point of an abscess, then the treatment with plaster remedies until it is healed.
des poilz des papieres	of the paper hairs
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hair begins to grow out of place instead of naturally and are aging, if they harm the eyes, and lead to conditions like accustomed tears and paper moistening and albuginea, as long as this is the cause of eye damage;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	And treatment takes place according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	And treatment can be carried out by means of a cautery and fire together, or through the use of remedies and potions as was discussed in the previous chapter on cautery, and this is done whether by incision and stitches, or by sutures, according to what I will explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary that you place the head of the patient in your healthy side, then turn the paper from your eye to your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	If it has been turned, that's good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	If not, then insert one needle with all the thread above;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	And either from the margin of the paper or where the hair grows beneath these hairs, and draw the thread above across the entire paper, and then turn it with the razor;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	Then place over the area on the paper, above the neatly arranged hairs, all across the broad chest to the small one.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then draw a line, and place on the paper a small cotton gauze tent and a piece of cloth, then draw a shape on the paper like an ivy leaf, as if it were a laurel tree, and always ensure that the shape corresponds to the height you see when lifting the paper which is marked for you.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if it's necessary to cover a large area of the paper according to how flexible the paper is;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then start from across the entire chest over the two lines you have marked, and begin at the broadest part of the chest down to the smallest.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	And make a cut near the natural hair openings in growth of a root, then place the onion in one of the two angles close to the ear, then burn completely.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	Then join the two lips with a stitch using a needle and all one strand of fine wool thread, and cleanse of blood, and burn off excess threads on the two ears for any sticky substances you see. If you do this properly;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	And if this does not work, then take no concern, let the stitch and threads until three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	Then treat the wound with dry and binding things, because paper gets wet from the heat of the wound and its joining, but stitches are damp (as the old ones said), and it's work without fear;
et si a une autre maniere:	And if there's another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	And it is that you seal the paper with a figure as round as an holly leaf, just like we have described, three inches square according to this shape:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then, cut those that are above evenly according to the shape shown here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you don't have the ability to hold the forceps, and if it's not equal, then take a needle or wherever there is thread, and stick it through the figure;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and thread another piece of wool through the large loop, and the second piece through the small one, and join the threads evenly between your thumbs;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift all the skin over which you have marked, just like we have described, then join the two edges of the wound by sewing, and treat until it heals.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	And if an abscess comes to your incision, soothe it with tallow and similar restorative balm;
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	And sometimes happens that the paper's hair gets converted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	It is necessary for you to use what we have instructed about incisions;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the stitches in one and the other are more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment for scabies follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and you must convert the paper and cut it internally according to what I have said. Then make two incisions with an art, and also make two fine threads as long as the paper is wide, taking into account its thickness;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and place two heads of each part where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	Then gather both together on what stands above the paper of the eye, and hold the two strings of each side firmly;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	And leave it like that for some days, and the skin which is being held will weaken, dry up, and peel off, until it falls out by itself.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it lasts longer, if the wound takes time to heal, then treat it as long as it remains healthy;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	And when the wound has healed, and if you lift off the paper, and no longer will grow hair;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the form of the two strings that you will make according to this shape, and according to this length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The operations are as follows: you take a fine needle and thread it with silk string that is strong and fine;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then gather together the shoulders and do not mix one with another subtly, and let the length of the threads be a palm in length;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then instruct in hunting another fine silk thread briefly, and tie the ends of the hair with this thread;
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then place the patient's head on your sound part;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And let the sunlight reach to all parts so that you can see clearly; because this is a delicate and small operation. Then thread the needle through all the hunting grounds at the base of the adjusted hair, and pierce it in the paper swiftly while you pull it above the natural hair.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then remove the hair up to the hunting ground, and thread that hair in the hunting ground, if there is one or two or three or more.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then remove your hand until the hairs grow out all around on paper with natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And when the chase is treated and the hair does not grow out with it, then remove the chase at the end to all the thread that you have ordered, until the chase grows out smoothly from almost above and you see this through the eye's vision;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Then remove the chase and the thread, and close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hair thickens in its place and grows the flesh out;
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are small, accompany them with one hair as long as a cow's hair, and lift it up alongside that or where you leave it, until it is fully grown out, then lift it.
de la porriture de l’oil	Regarding eye infection
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this illness, called "aleacrati" or gangrene comes to the eye, if there are two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One naturally, and the other unnaturally.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And occurs suddenly from injury, or due to surgeons, or by means of cauterization, and through similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way of treatment in this is that you cut open this seam and expose the eyelid, and place linen wicks inside, and keep it until it has healed;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And it is not right to use in the treatment of this any things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the illness will return worse than the first one;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but work with things that soften, such as fennel;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and wash it with hot water or vinegar and linseed oil, and apply onion juice in none of the oils, and cover it with a linen cloth, and treat it with this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And remember when healing, you must guard against the wound not mending according to its original form;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And these remedies that we have discussed apply only to this disease, so that it does not return according to its original form.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	The flow that comes to the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease which truly is called 'axacrati', and it occurs naturally due to accidents.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accidents come from wounds and tears, from cauterization, and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	And the method of performing this operation involves inserting an awl with a doubled thread into the skin, threading it through and piercing just to the left of the right eyelid as far as you can reach inwards, so that the thread goes through two layers of tissue;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then the skin is held above all along the awl, and it's cut wide over the spur.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the figure of the paper returns according to what is proper, it is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If not, then seize it with care and place it in the groove, and turn the paper, and make two cuts where they would have been inside the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	Make the two corners of the two cuts corresponding to the two angles of the incision you made, and make the angles such that when they are assembled together, the figure will be like the figure of a letter that is "Greek";
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	Then set the bone according to the quantity that its thicknesses require, following the size of the paper hole, then adjust the two required parts and sew them with a thread line's length.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply the cure as we have said about softening medicines and treatments, until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from a wound or seam or cautery, then it is necessary that you cut an opening filled with hair on the paper, and according to what was mentioned before;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then dig between the two rows of a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And one must do the work according to the shape of the disease, for it is very diverse in its form, and the wise surgeons arrange themselves with all their skills to show how they can return the shape to its natural form;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And even the patients themselves, according to what needs to be done and with various instruments in many arrangements.
dou soudement de la papiere	immediately from the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this sewing occurs with people's hands in such a manner that the paper above is glued with the white of the oil and cannot move or perform its natural tasks, then it is necessary to poke the tip of a scraper under the paper and lift it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	And the length should be as pins, until you find the one that is inserted into the subtle sphenoid bone, which should not be too large or too sharp, so that the patient does not suffer from a needle that is too large and stings the eye;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	And make your incision, by which you excise the assembled tissue lightly, so that the paper heals according to its natural form;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	And heal all the assembled tissue, and perform no piercing in the sharp eyesight, but lift with mild water and from a basin;
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	Then place between the paper and the eye a linen tent, and put damp wool on top of the eye from an egg's content;
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	And after three days, use mild water and other bland substances until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	Of the edge of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that the nail occurs in two manners:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	It occurs in two ways: one is nervous and seems like hard bone, and another that isn't nerve-filled but appears like white moist lump frozen over, such that when iron is touched to it and cared for with the use of prongs, it won't move.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	Both kinds start near the large tear duct and grow gradually until they cover all of the eye and all light and vision.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the method of incision is such that the patient positions their head over your hand, then they pull out the eyes.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and hold the paper in your hand, then pinch the nail with small prongs, and stretch it upwards.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and attach a horse hair, or a calf hair, or a cow hair, and strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the needle point and insert it into the nail bed, then pierce through the entire needle, and bind the nail with a thread and extend it above, and burn all the hair on the nail bed that surrounds the artery and the fine hairs until the root of the cuticle in the fleshy part under the nail bed. Then cut out the remaining parts along the groove up to the sensitive subcutaneous tissue and small muscles, and leave the natural tear, so that no liquid comes out like usual through the incision.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	And each time, the nail is extended only to the edge and with thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then for the scorched one, remove all the burnt flesh from which this is made:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And see to it that no more of the burnt flesh touches the fatty tissue and doesn't tear it, and that the wound does not become punctured;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	After making the incision, pour a little of the broiled fat into it, and create a ring from stearine, and let it heal until tomorrow;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat those who require it as long as they are sound.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not nerve-filled, and you cannot push the needle through it, and the cuticles cannot enter, this kind of nail-like condition is treated many times with medicinal remedies;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	And it happens just as I described in the division, and if you see that it is coped, let the eye work with the help of the diseased flesh, take out a small amount of burnt flesh gently according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And raise the nail slightly, and if you see that it is not diminishing at all and your reason presses on, then from your mouth, pour into the eye ring made of stannous oxide and red necklace and yellow fluid onto the eye until the next day.
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	Then repeat the other operation according to this same work, until it is completely removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing obstructs your view, such as pus-filled sores, then proceed, and first treat the pus-filled sores until they are clean. Then resume the work procedure just described, until they are clean.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the cheek of the eye, by great discomfort, appears in the eye at night, then suspend it under a gurney, and take out a part of it, not all at once, so that no tears come from it;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then pour into the red eye ring which is made of stannous oxide.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	Of the flesh that grows near the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	There are some men who never pass urine red, and covers the pupil and remains on the papers, and turns outside, appearing as a candle flame;
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the operations are such that the patient places their head in your hand, then guide their eyes, and all that flesh up to the bone is brought down to sizes suitable for this, and you hold it with strength;
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then cut the first layer of flesh, and saw everything down to the bone until the end, and be sure not to hurt the eye in the operation.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the cut be like what we described in cutting nails and using small force of your hands, just like the figure shown after this chapter regarding bone separation;
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the cut is done and all flesh has been separated, use oil of sulfur or distill it with red colander-like medicine, and place a cotton ball soaked in such substance on top of the wound to prevent infection;
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	And if it remains unchanged, and the person with no shoes surmounts you, and you doubt over an abscess in such a case, then let the eye and treat the abscess using remedies that soothe such an abscess.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work until it is healed, and thus make as many characters as are attached by this resemblance in the eye.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, nevertheless, it is necessary that you adapt the treatment of each natural weakness in the eye;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and from the accidental path, in the work of iron;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	And do not let your hand stay in any of these works until you see that this limb endures the pain of this operation.
des voines des eulz	of veins and eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	When the veins are red and covered above the eye, and affect vision, causing weakeness in sight for several days.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	Therefore, the first skill is to observe where the eye is, and from which side, and apart from that, there is no other disease except for the boil;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	Therefore treat him in this way:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Instruct the patient to place his head in a healthy position, then suspend all vessels throughout the entire body according to their wisdom, and let the arteries be twofold subtly as this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And let there be two inches by degree in one side according to this shape:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	Then treat that way forcefully suspending those subtle vessels, and let blood flow for an hour after another, until you see the vessels leaving the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And ensure that you don't pierce the eye at the tips of the spathamides, and perform this operation at midday in front of the sun, and be very zealous in your work so that you do not cause injury only to those vessels.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, if you distill in the eye a collar of green and red to corrupt what remains stubborn against the blow.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you do not have the power to do all this at once, make a poultice on the eye with things that calm the pain of the eyes and leave it for several days until the pain is soothed and sure there's no pus in it, then restart according to this method as described until they are healed;
et c’est li forme des forces:	And it is the shape of strength:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the tear duct of the eye
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The method for something called "arissati" is a fistula:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you cure it with a cautery and with hot medicinal fluids as I have said before, and if it's not yet healed, then it remains within the place where you incise on the pus, near where it should die. Drain all the moisture that is there, until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when you see the bone has been exposed, and you will notice the decay and darkness, if you retrieve with all the instrument which was previously described;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and is called 'hard head', and made of iron, directed towards the head region, and should be sharpened like a file as it appears in its current form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place on it the part of the decaying bone, then turn it with your fingers, and press your hand a little until you know that this corruption has stopped;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this once, then restore the head to its state of medicinal desiccation.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	if the bones are joined, and flesh has begun to grow, and the skin of the wound is joined, and remains like this for forty days, and does not heal or become an abscess, and no bad incidents occur, know that it is healed.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not this, so other means must be used to bring back the fistula to its proper place at the tip of the nail according to this form:

si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it's something lighter for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	from the exit of the eye

de la bowe de l’oil	By the power of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease which is called "alcunnati" can only be found where bile is present in the gallbladder, resembling falling drops of water, and it is not real water;

des aigues de l’oil	From the drops of the eye
