et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	And these forms and others prepare with you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	When treating someone for tooth pain, it is necessary to draw out the tooth as much as you can while delaying its extraction, because this should not cause them any harm.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	because it is such a high substance that one would not have any excuse for piercing it.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Therefore, when the patient is compelled to strain for the extraction, it is necessary that you are certain of which tooth is causing pain.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain leads to the body, and be sure that it is or a tooth, and extract the good tooth;
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	yet still do not leave the pain alone during this time, until the bad tooth is removed, for we have already wished to do so with these soldiers;
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	And when you are certain about the tooth that is causing pain, it is necessary to burn inside of the tooth with quite a large amount of spittle in order to preserve the gum from all sides;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then move to your hands or take hold of the delicate forceps at the first pinch and pinch again, until they are well dislocated, then firmly secure the forceps.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and have the shoulder under the knee in your holy place between your knees, and hold it well so that it doesn't move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the right tooth correctly without breaking it, and if it does not jump out forcefully, take no concern with these instruments and gently push them in from each side. And move it just like you did initially.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if they have pierced and eaten through it, then you must fill with cloths where the holes are;
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and when using delicate forceps to hold it, make sure not to break it during the holding.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	And one must cut quite carefully under the gum to extract the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And see to it well that you don't break it and leave a piece behind; this will cause the patient even greater pain due to the malady of the root.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And beware that you do not do it as the ignorant surgeons do, who break the bone every time out of haste and audacity, and do not carry out what we have told.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	But they cause to occur from time to time by the opening of this great disease through their roots that they bear, or through the matter they break, as we have often found;
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	And when the flesh is torn, wash the part with wine or ale and salt;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	And when blood leakage occurs, which often happens, cover the area with roasted vitriol;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	And if that doesn't work, apply cautery.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The shapes of the tools you use to remove teeth should be those with long points and thick handles, so that they do not bend when you pull out a tooth;
et ce sont les formes:	And these are the shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And let them have large parts that do not bend when being pulled, and be made of very sturdy iron, and should have teeth to hold the pieces in place.
de la racine des dens	from the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains at the draw, it is necessary to place cotton soaked in moist butter inside the wound for one or two days until the wound softens. Then pinch the tweezers called 'algefri', by which the blood seems like that of a well-tended animal;
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and they should be as fine as a file and this is the shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out with all these forceps, it is necessary that you uncover the entire mass right up to the root, and then place an instrument known as 'althali', which is essentially an awl, as depicted here:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And make it strong and thick so that it doesn't break, and if the root jumps out due to this, it is good;
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	if not, assist with all your tools, of which the descriptions follow:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if assistance is taken from the instrument that has two points, as depicted here:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other tools that are in front according to the size of teeth, and from this tool which seems like large forceps, as depicted here:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And make these instruments strong so they don't break, and know that many tools are used inside;
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	And also other instruments, which are not counted;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	And the wise surgeons discover their instrument by themselves, according to what their operations and illnesses demonstrate to them. For there are diseases where old men did not teach an instrument due to the diversity of these and they break part from the carriage or others' bones, or if it rots away, then he seeks out the instruments that suit him, which I have told you about, and helps with movements, whose form is this:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And be thick and well-suited to hold onto the bone, so that it doesn't slip away, but can hold and remove it;
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	and then restore the limb using suitable medications for this, and if there is rot in the bone, and it is small, if she retrieves all of her instrument:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the teeth seem not according to the body's natural course, and their form is ugly, even in virginal women, you must know if they were born after a tooth and are not in its right place, and cannot be seen or shaved.
adonques lou raie;	Therefore, the tooth;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	And if it is next to the tooth, take this tool described here, and it resembles a small beak, and it should be made of sharp iron.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the hole is made small and smaller in my hands by its hardness due to tooth, and because you do not move others, and if it becomes apparent that one can shave it off, then I will shave with one piece of file as this forms:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and is also like the file used to make needles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and gradually file down the tooth bit by bit with gentle hand movements, so that it doesn't move until it finishes;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	Then smooth it in the end for any rough edges, and if the tooth is too sharp and hurts the tongue, you should file down the roughness until it's level, so that it doesn't hurt the tongue or impair speech.
quant li dent lochent	When the tooth swells
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the teeth in front of the mouth, through impact or bite, and if the patient can't push on it while eating without vomiting, and you have treated them with restraining medicines, then this is not effective;
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	if you need to restrict them with an gold thread, because the silver threads turn green and rot, but the gold never changes;
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and make the thread neither too thick nor too thin, according to the size of the space between the teeth;
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you see the teeth moving, take the thread and double it between the two healthy teeth, then place the dislocated teeth between the diseased ones, whether there is one or more than one, as long as you can feel them safely up to a healthy tooth on the other side;
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	Then restart the covering until you reach the part where you stopped, and apply your skilled and gentle hand pressure, without letting it move at all.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and make sure to bind around the tooth root so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then clip the threads with some forceps, and join them together, placing them between healthy teeth, and place them in such a way that they do not irritate the tongue;
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	and leave it that way as tight as can be tolerated, and if it loosens or the threads break, apply a different thread to tighten again;
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	if it can be tolerated for its entire duration, and this is the form of teeth and the position of the two healthy incisors and the two premolars as you see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth is withdrawn, if it is placed back in its position, time after time, as we have said;
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and don't interfere with any that aren't experienced and endure it, and not once do we shape a bone tooth like that of a cow, and place it in the spot where the defect is, and hold it firmly as we have said, and remains and serves for so long.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	To cover the tie of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Not once does a tongue lien come from underneath the tongue or jaw, that one is born like this;
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by mistake due to a healed wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the procedures are such that you work on the mouth with the patient, have their head in your healthy position, and lift the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	Then cut the nerve link in the middle, as long as the tongue is dislocated from its place. And if there is hardness or swelling, and it's due to sudden injury, should you break the hook and cut the larger link.
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	And make sure that the wound is not too wide at the base, for there is an artery beneath it;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	And once done, if you have used water that is pinkish and warm or cool, then place the head in a container of cold water. Afterward, put a linen tent under the tongue;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	And let the patient's wounds be treated every night, so that no pus may accumulate.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if there is blood drainage, then put vinegar under the head;
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	And if it doesn't respond to you, then apply the gentle cautery, which is suitable for such cases;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	then apply another treatment until it becomes clear,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	and if you see it is of a red or black or hard color, yet the patient does not feel it, do not touch it, for this is a gangrene;
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	and if it is draining pus and there's moisture, let the honey flow, and apply a thin needle cut, and relieve from both sides;
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	and if it doesn't respond to your treatment, while you're working on it, put sulfur ash until it is coated, then return to your work until you use up all the strength;
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then raise up the patient from bed and from rest, and continue other treatments while they are well.
des apostemes de la gorge	Extractions from the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	No sickness enters the throat glands which are called 'godath', and they should be properly referred to as the second pair of lymph nodes. And when you treat them, as we have explained in the division, if they are still inflamed, take care:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If it's hard pus with small sensation and is colored, don't touch it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it's red and the root is large, don't touch it with iron either, for the running of blood;
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	but let it be until it heals, and then you will remove it, or it would burst on its own;
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it has a pale white color and the root is subtle, if you prepare your instrument to cover, but first check that the abscess's swelling rests and has calmed.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Therefore, have the patient sit facing the sun, and let their head be in good health, and make them open their mouth and place your forefinger between their hands on the tongue, pressing it towards all the instrument, as this is its form;
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	And may be made of fine silver or very sharp like knives:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	Can you press the tongue onto this entire instrument, and see the abscess? If so, take an onion and a thorn, and drive them in from above more forcefully than you can.
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	And take nothing off the skin with it, then grasp the object with the tool, from which there is this shape, that seems like some strength;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	And always the head is curved and one place to another, and they are very sharp, and it is made of iron or steel:
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you don't have this tool now, take scissors instead; in this way it is formed:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And be sharp on one side, and the other unnamed;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And when you have gripped one of the kidneys, grip the other in the same manner, and after incision gargle the wounds with hot, then cold water, or with both hot and cold water. If bleeding occurs during this process, gargle with hot water, or use cooked pomegranate peels or rosemary leaves, among similar things, until the wound is fully healed;
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then continue the treatment as long as he remains healthy;
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	And no more abscesses form in the throat than there were two almonds, if they grow like so with exactly two almond-sized lumps.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman for an abscess that was born within her throat, this being known as the small airway abscess;
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	And it had almost completely blocked the entire throat, so that the woman could not breathe through the constricted passage and could neither eat nor drink, she died if she had continued like this for a day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	And the abscesses was so high that it had forced to make two holes through both nostrils near the nose.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I acted quickly then, and inserted an instrument in the one inch opening, after which the straw came out, and with great force was a large portion of the food expelled.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	Then I would proceed to cut another piece near its other nostril, and open the wound with my knife and force the tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	After inserting the needle into these abscesses, and removing some of them, only a little blood came out.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	And thus, the woman's throat passage was opened, and she began to drink water and then wine from now on. I didn't stop cutting out from that abscess for a long time;
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	And the abscesses would reoccur immediately, filling up almost the entire cavity that I had emptied, until it became quite large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	And then I would insert something and cauterize inside the throat:
ensi demora sens croistre;	So it didn't grow further;
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	And I leave these parts, may God have mercy on him after me.
de l’uve	Of the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When it bends towards the eye, and it has lengthened and become elongated, this is called "perpendicular";
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	And if it becomes swollen and round, it's called an "eye".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it is treated as we have described in the section on treatment, and if the treatment doesn't help, and you notice that the pus from the abscess has subsided, and there's a thin layer left, then it's necessary to remove it;
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	And that which is round and not elongated;
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	And if it's red or reddish or black in color, then it's necessary to make an incision into it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For there is great danger for the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	Therefore, when you see it, according to the manner that I have said, concerning its shape and length, you should have the patient face the sun, and press the tongue with the instrument about which we have made mention previously.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then place the onion in the stomach and treat it there, and cover it with the two instruments that I mentioned for incising the kidneys.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And it is necessary that you do not cover more than the excess which is beyond the natural limit;
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	because if you cover too much, you harm the voice and speech.
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And after making an incision, use what we have discussed for the incision of the two kidneys, and treat her until she is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the patients are afraid of the cut, it is necessary for you to use remedies for the cautery of the sensitive area.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	And the way of the cautery is like boiling water.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And it is that the patient should place their head in your good health, and then press their tongue against the tool we have described or the cautery chapter's instructions, and secure it with sharp blades, so that they are not too thick nor too thin.
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	and by using the power of this tool, which is described here:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And let your head bear a hair or where you apply the medicine, like how spoons do it, and place the tool with all the medicine over the wound;
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	And let the patient stay still on their side, so that saliva and mucus flow from their mouth into the medicine, but not down to the throat, and rinse;
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	Then hold your hand with all the medicine and press it on the wound for half an hour, as long as you see it seeping out and the patient's reactions to the medicine are calmed;
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	And if you see this, take cotton and wrap it around any tool, and moisten the cotton in the medicine, then cover the tool with all the cotton on top of the canvas, until the cotton burns out on the surface.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	And do this often, until the cauterization is perfect, then leave it to dry, and remove it after three or five days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you need to repeat the cauterization with the medicinal preparation, do it again, and after the cauterization, rub inside the surface of the wound with cotton stuffed in butter, and clean what is inside from the medicine;
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And rinse with cold water, or perform gargling treatments until it heals.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is safer than incision, just using the cauterization;
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	If it is treated with fumigation in this way, take calamus and myrrh and oregano and rue and chamomile and borage and similar herbs, and gather them all or some of them into a pot, and place them there, and bring the water to a boil;
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	and let the pot be well filled with strong earth, and in the middle of the pot place the burning instrument according to this manner:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And let it be made of silver or lead, and let one of the shoulder blades be placed in the mouth of the patient until the vapor rises through the nose by way of the throat, as long as the urethra is necrotic;
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	After it repeats often, as long as the urethra dries, and remember that you should not do this at the beginning of the formation of pus, for many things happen;
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	And do not use this force when removing an abscess tip.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not present, take a feather and place an eggshell inside the patient's head, so that the mouth of the diseased area does not get too hot;
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	for the eggshell does not produce a thick steam in the mouth, and this is a good combination for healing together with health.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times there is air in the throat bone or spine of fish, or no thing;
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	Therefore, you should extract what you can see, and press the tongue to the sun with all the instrument, so that you see the thing move;
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	And what does not open and is stuck in the throat, you should make the patient vomit this way that the meat be cooked in the stomach;
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	By chance if by vomiting the substance comes out;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	or it is when the patient swallows an sponge piece, or a navel piece, or a lettuce root, or a fragment of dry bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	and attaches to the sponge a thread, and then swallows it;
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	and when it reaches its place, if it inflates, and then draws out force;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if it does not come out with what we have said, take an instrument of plunge according to this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the instruments be curved towards the head so that it can enter the throat more easily, and have the head raised to the top;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	and beware not to touch the epiglottis, that all may go well, nor to push any bone inside;
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	And it is necessary for the patient to hold onto the tool, because if it moves or if the thing being treated becomes dry;
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	If the tool is placed inside, or it is pulled forcefully to all parts of the instrument equally, as long as it is forceful.
de la sansue de la gorge	of the windpipe
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	No treatment heals without fluids, just as I have explained in the division, by medication cure;
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	And when this does not help, then look at the throat of the patient towards the sun, and press the tongue with the instrument I have told you.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	And if you see the vein, guide it with all small inch, or with fine forceps that are worth this.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if that doesn't work, take a thread and apply it in the neck next to the patient's wound, then move or pull on the thread until you feel resistance, and do this frequently.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And if you irrigate the patient with water throughout the day.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	Then take full sight of cold water, and work the mouth, and pour it into senses to swallow, and move it often with her hand;
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	And if soon the fluids smell the water, she will defecate.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	And if it does not behave as we have said, then fumigate the patient with asafetida, using the tool that I mentioned for the fumigation of the eye.
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	Do this multiple times, because it will expel without causing harm.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	And the method of fumigation is as follows: take a pan with charcoal briquettes, and place it covered with a perforated lid in the middle, and at this opening you place the tool's head.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	Then pour the fumigation, and the patient puts the tip of the rod in their mouth, and closes their mouth so that no smoke escapes but only goes up to the nose.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	And now the nostril will expel (the contents), and if it does not happen, repeat the fumigation multiple times.
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	And the patient suffers thirst, and eats dirty things and such, and does not drink water;
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	And then it is necessary for her to come out through this governance.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the shape of the tool with which we treat the sanguine matter, when it can be seen, resembles curved tongs meant to enter the throat;
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	And it has the appearance of a doctor's beak, and it has the roughness of a file, in such a way that whatever she takes, she cannot leave.
et vez ci la forme:	And here is the form:
li chapistres des apostemes	The chapter on abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	There are no descriptions of discharges until memory brings it forward from one or the other in this book, and they differ in puncturing and shaping;
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	And this is through two ways; one being in its likeness itself, and concerning the one that holds moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second way is for those limbs which are inside the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	For the abscesses of the head are different from those of the base, and the abscesses of the internal organs differ from those that come to joints, and each has its judgment in action.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And if it comes to discharges, one should not pierce them until the wound is healed according to its completion;
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	And for those that must be pierced when they are matured and do not heal according to their completion, such as discharges within joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	For when abscesses come from joints and they are allowed to continue until they become purulent internally, by chance, if the ligament and nerve of the joint get corrupted, this is a cause for contraction in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	If the discharge is within the main limb, and if you delay piercing until it is dead, it will harm the main limb;
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	Or if it's within the foundation, piercing it or so long as it is dead;
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	And it is not right that you pierce a mature discharge without full digestion completed, except for the one that's within the foundation where it can burn internally and result in an ongoing tunnel;
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	And cannot heal completely.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	And you should know the time for draining the abscess which is determined by completion, and this occurs when the pain has subsided, and the departure of fever, and the reduction in pain and redness, and during the movement and improvement of the head of the abscess, and other signs.
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	And you should keep the draining area or further depending on the location of the abscess, and where it opens will move.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	And let the drainage be along the length of the arrow, and if the abscess is on the limbs or in joints and necks and arteries, and everywhere where there is no pleating.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In these cases, when they bend, according to that limb.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when abscesses are in the living tissue, it is better to let the puncturing happen until digestion is fully completed, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	For if you pierce it in front of that, it will lengthen the arrow with its venom and is full of maggots;
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	And by chance harden the lips and weaken him from within.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And if there are no abscesses pierced straight through the center of the body as per need for each limb.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	It is necessary that you remove small pus blisters, small wounds;
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	And in large blisters, large wounds, and many cuts according to the size of the blister;
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	And if there are such blisters or if it is necessary to cover with lard, and cover;
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	when it has become as soft as leather, and is flattened out, then one should do as is done with infants:
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	And for those that split into three corners, and those that are cut like the leaf of myrtle, like blisters from angles;
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	And for those where one makes a round cut, and other cuts and appearances of cutter.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	Those who do not have a head, such as abscesses located superficially, it must be that you pierce them completely;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	And when the abscesses are large, and they have accumulated a great amount of pus, you must pierce them, but do not drain all the pus at once in that moment, but drain part of it;
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	Then apply an ointment over the abscess until another day, then do nothing until it heals;
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	Repeat this process several times gradually, until all the pus has drained out.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	Similarly, if the patient lacks strength, or is pregnant, or has small children, or elderly and weak individuals.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For when someone tries to force it with the expulsion of blood, sometimes causing death of the patient, and you do not realize this.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	Therefore, proceed with caution in this chapter. When you have pierced your abscess, if a wound appears, and check to see if the wound from the abscess is small;
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	And if it's a flat iron, you may try using linen or raw cotton thread.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	And if it's a large abscess and there are many wounds, you need to puncture each one so that they press against each other;
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	And if you have incised in the abscess and sewed it internally, you should fill it with old cotton or linen rags without moisture and bind it up to the first joint;
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then proceed with the bone and treat with ointment until it is sound.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if blood leakage occurs in your operation, then apply cold and ease, and moist with cloths, and place it in the operated area repeatedly.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	And if the bleeding persists, you should apply treatment and care, and use the powders that I have mentioned in this book; if it's or ten of a feather, and the patient is suffering greatly from bleeding, then it would be good to place moistened cloths and bandages on them using wine and heated oil.
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if it's in this state, and the limbs are fatty, you should immerse them in wet cloths soaked in water and oil, or in wine and cold oil, until three days have passed, as we said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then remove and clean the abscess, following the proper procedures, until it is healed.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	And one should know universally about treating abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	Or I have told you how to proceed before treating abscesses, and here is the chapter.
des soros	regarding the surgical treatment
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	For some small ulcers come from the head, and are in our style as they are on cloths, like a blemish on a rabbit's hide, and there are many that resemble.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	There are some that are fatty and others where moisture is also like peas;
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	And for those that are hard and stony to the knife, there is no doubt that they are arteries and do not oppose.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the actions of cutting are that you should try with all the instrument which is called "entromissor", from whose form comes this afterward, what it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	For if it contains moisture, you make the incision over its length.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when moisture is expelled, one must not leave anything behind the skin containing that moisture, for it immediately returns when nothing is left.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	then dip cotton in Egyptian ointment, if it's available;
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	if not that, then in water and salt, and apply it to the wound, leaving it until the next day;
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	and this will help someone who is affected by night demons.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And continue with the cotton, just as before, on the second day and the third, until you can tell clearly that it doesn't stay affected by night.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with an ointment suitable for it, until it heals properly.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if an abscess holds tightly within him, you should remove it according to this form, long;
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	and empty out your ashes, and scorch all around, and apply all your healing strength to the area where it is located;
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	and if the artery goes against you, then do what I have told you to do afterward.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And similarly, deal with the abscess if it's due to stones, and when cutting and treating, do as I have instructed.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And when it comes to cutting on stone-caused abscesses and dampness, the operation is lighter because there's less blood involved.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if in any of these abscesses or head where there is no moisture, and for these old-style abscesses that I mentioned or the head of an elderly woman;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	and found the abscess to be as hard as a dense stone, rough and white, and could not break it;
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	and if any were cut open, we would have made the wound as well as from a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	For other abscesses coming near the head, if they come near the heads of children and the roots of the ears, the incision should be made for all days at the earliest possible time, so that the blood may exit.
et les cure si com il covient.	and the treatment as it should be done.
des scrophules	Of scrofula
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	Many times such abscesses occur at the neck, and in the throat, and near the jaws, and never come to any other part or on a body, they are round, and are bound together.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	And each sore is properly within its socket, like the node and the abscess near the head, as we have said;
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	And the appearances of these sores are many.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	There are some that contain moisture, and there are others that don't want to comply with health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	In such cases where you see good positioning on the neck, and appears similar to the color of the chest, it is mute from both sides and not mixed under the collarbone nor near the artery or in the channel, and is not deeply seated;
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	If it is necessary that you handle it from above, and burn each part, and keep the two lips close to their original shape when necessary, just like we have explained with abscesses on the head;
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	And do it slowly and carefully, be sure not to touch the nerve or vein, nor should there be too much bleeding or cutting, that your hands don't escape, and don't see too far ahead, so you don't treat more than what you should.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you treat the vein or artery and it doesn't allow you to open, then apply vitriol or some powders that stop blood, and restrain the wound;
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	And let it be until the abscesses are calmed and the wound becomes soft, then begin to rot it.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when the patient has recovered from their illness, return to your work, as long as you finish it;
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	And if there remain any small scabs, if they scratch and clean them out.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if the root of the pimple is large, it is not suitable to pinch that pimple at its root, but tie a thick double thread around it and let it hang down without causing harm;
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then use old cotton dipped in Egyptian ointment, then the treatment.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	And if you cure all the scrophula, it is necessary that you join together the two lips of the wound, and suture now, because there is no excess to remain due to the size of the scrophula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	It is necessary that you understand how to cut into it and drain the pus, and then sew up afterwards as we have said.

de squinance	"De squinance" in this context refers to treatments or procedures related to diseases or deformities of the neck and head region. This could cover a variety of topics such as injuries, infections, tumors, dislocations, and other medical conditions affecting these areas. Without more context from the specific text you're referring to, it's difficult to provide an exact translation for each line in this term. However, generally speaking, "squinance" implies a focus on neck-related ailments or surgery.
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The old ones told and spoke about the surgery of the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	but I never saw anyone in our land perform it, and this is their written word.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	For those with strabismus, it is necessary that the incision of the throat known as "the epiglottis" be made;
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	yet do not underestimate this, because all the veins and the lung of the disease are in those with abscesses either within the mouth or in the throat or between the two lungs.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the disease is in the channel of the windpipe, it is necessary to cover the epiglottis to prevent loss from strangulation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	Therefore, when we wish to cut the epiglottis, we should cut it through three or four small incisions across, between the two circles, or by the size of the incision in relation to its depth, not in the cartilage.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	And these joints are amenable to the cutting of the epiglottis where there is no flesh, and the vessel extends deep within.

puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then administer medicines which promote growth of flesh, as long as they heal.

Albucasim insists that one should not stop this process until the throat is completely swollen and the patient is pronounced dead, and until all deficiencies are met.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Therefore treat the epiglottis because the patient cannot eat or drink, and they breathe through the wound, so thus precautions should be taken against death;

I discovered the wound and found the blood coming from it, indeed, she did not have a cut vein or artery leading there but the veins were flowing through the wound.
