li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	Let the two shoulders be held and cut, and let the shoulders also be as large as the elbows equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error in the world's creation lies when the intestines escape at the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, it is necessary for you to extend up to your finger-tip, so that the intestines can be released;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And treat them equally, and if you cannot hold it by your fingernail, then use tweezers, and then treat it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they penetrate for three days, and the one who is on the verge swells up, you should let it be until the abscesses are soothed, and gently scrape lightly.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	If you can move it like that, and keep the part of the penis untouched, this will not harm it at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Therefore, cure the wound from sudden injuries with powder, as we have said or treated with powders. And if you cut too roughly and it goes beyond, this will not harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Cure him accordingly, as we have said, while he remains sound.
dou retenement de l’urine	holding back of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	Retention of urine can be due to a stone obstruction, or frozen blood, or bowel blockage, or internal bleeding, or other such conditions we have discussed in the section;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if their urine is not being relieved, and you see that it is being retained due to a stone or blockage in the bladder's neck, then it would be proper for the patient to squat with their knees raised;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And have them place their feet on the back, and extend their belly from the area above the back, and restrain the patient so they can barely stand.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And then the necks of the bladder are constrained towards the expression of the stone above, so that urine is relieved.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you should administer extraction with all the instrument which is called "syringe", of which here is its form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	And let it be of fine silver, barely a hair's breadth, like the feathers of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	Let it be the length of a palm and a half, and let it be fine at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the way of the passage of urine is such that you take a double thread, and tie it at the end of some wool or cotton, and insert the tip of the needle inside the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And cut off the excess of the wool and insert it up to the tip of the needle, then smear the needle with oil or butter and beaten egg yolk, and have the patient sit down, and wet the bladder and the penis with oily olive oil and tepid water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then gently insert the syringe into the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the bladder.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe until it reaches just before the bladder, and feel the patient urinate until they are empty, and this is not done according to this order because for him who guides her to where she was twisted;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch the thread all along with a gentle tug, and let the urine follow the thread, then pull it out gently, and ensure proper urine flow.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And continue using the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and ensure that the patient urinates properly.
des maladies de la vessie	About diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or blood come to the bladder, or putrefaction is assembled there, and you see waters and medicines distilling, if make everything for the tool called 'clepsis' (an ancient water measure), and its form is:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It's sealed, and if there are three parts:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	On one side, and on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	And if you are among those for whom medical care is as such that it makes the member feel well without addition, so long as there's no moisture and expulsion when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you see the medicine being discharged into the bladder, place the patient in moisture, and apply to the one who is in charge;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	If you remove the moisture from the penis, then firmly set the one in charge again.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	And if moisture enters him now and reaches the bladder, then the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	This is the form of subtle colic in which one treats the bladder with colic.
si est ci:	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or iron, and the shoulder blade rises higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and reaches up to the spine or the neck of the shoulder blade;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a lamb bladder and fill it with moist heat that you see in the process of preparing the bladder, then tie it between the two shoulders using a good pair of twine, and heat one end of this moist heat on fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then conduct the bladder through the catheter into the vagina, then hold your hand on the bladder until all the moist heat has been applied, as long as the patient feels that this moist heat has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	And if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make a circle, then pierce it roundly through;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	Then bind a strong thread in these bends, then form the circle as you would a hoop, and put inside what you see of dirt, moisture and water, and tie it to the tool;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And do it like you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until moisture accumulates in the bladder.
de la piere	Of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have discussed methods of stone extraction and combined treatments;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	And we have explained the differences between stones that obstruct the flow of urine and all the symptoms, and when one should open for size;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	And in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	And I will explain it clearly and briefly to you.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that stones that are obstructed in the bladder occur more often in children, and this is a sign that the fever jumps from the bladder similar to fever by its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	And when you open the wound, and scrape the patient's genitals, and do this many times, and then reassemble.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and at the mouth of these jumps there is support;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and there is easy healing of children until they are four years old, and there is much complaint among the elderly, and it is midway, for those who are between childhood and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and healing is easier for those with larger stones than for those with smaller ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to treatment, it is necessary first to purify the patient by fasting, in order to drain out all the bile which is within the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it clogs up one way or another when seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take hold of the patient by their testicles and lift them up, moving downwards so that the stone descends to the front of the bladder, and does not protrude from anywhere above.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have the patient sit between your hands with their arms extended outward, so that the bladder is fully descending downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	Then touch and probe inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in space, if you hurry now, cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it doesn't feel like it's at all under the toucher, moisten your index finger of your left hand, if the patient is young, or your middle finger, if the patient is old.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	And dig into its foundation, probe the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, pull it at the neck of the bladder.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	Then press on your finger, and dig outward from where you see to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the surgeon to press the bladder with their hand, and command them to extend their arms up with their right hand, and with their left hand hold the skin near the penis in the area where one would make a cut.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then I remove the swollen spleen, whose form is this:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And they make in that which is between the kidneys and the foundation, not in the middle but at the edge of the left kidney's area.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And let it be straight on the stone, and may your tool touch or be at the foundation, and make its size through such that it's wide outside and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	By chance if your tool that is at the foundation jumps senseless during work;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	And know that there's stone or it has edges and margins:
si est griés a issir;	If it gets stuck to come out;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And if it's part that is under, resembles a gallbladder, and round, whose output is light.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	In the place where there are angles and margins, make the opening larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it doesn't jump out, you should use forceps that are shaped like a file at the end, for to apply pressure on the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you press against it with the tip of the subtle curved instrument at its base;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you can't use it like that, make it slightly wider but not too much thick, and if the stone is hard, apply it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there are more than one stone, first take the larger one from the neck of the bladder, then move upwards, then use force, and the smaller ones after if there are more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if she is very large, then it suits to sever, and create a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	or he dies, or his urine starts coming out immediately when his legs can't be sewn together;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but strive to treat it or use forceps until you remove it piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, if you treat the wound with incense and aloes and dragon's blood, compress it, apply it topically, or place a wet cloth on it soaked in oil and wine, or oil and cold water and rose water, to soothe the inflamed area;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then straighten the patient's back and do not release the ligament until three days have passed.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you untie it, wash the area well with oil and water, then apply the dyafinicon ointment and basilico ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if abscesses come into the wound and cause corrosion, and blood clots in the bladder, and thus retain his urine, which is known to occur like this without jumping with urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Therefore, you must clean the wound, and remove that blood, for if it remains, it will corrode the bladder, and it will rot.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then clean the wound from water and slime and dirt, and assist with all methods you know, until it is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and ensure that every time you treat him, you tie the two legs together, and apply medicine to the wound.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it's located where the penis leads out, stuck in there, so that the urine cannot come out;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if you treat him as I have described, cut him many times, and forgive the loss of length due to this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I already have this experience like this.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron twig according to this form, and have it with three points stuck into one stake:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take thread and tie it around the penis near the stone, so that it does not come back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then bend the twig gently on the penis until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and twist the twig in your hand at the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from elsewhere;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	if urine starts to come out, then press your hand on the one that is stuck from the stone which is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it breaks soon, and jump with urine, and beware of the patient;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie a string under the stone and another above, then place the penis between the two strings in the area of the stone, then pull hard, and remove the string, and cleanse the congealed blood in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat until it becomes healthy.
de la piere des femmes	From the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	Sometimes stones get stuck in women, and if it happens once, the treatment is strict, and it is forbidden for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One reason is perhaps that the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	And the second reason is that one cannot find women who know how to hide themselves even when they are chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third way is that perhaps one cannot find women who know this skill of hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth way is that the stone in a woman might be larger than a man's stone, so it requires a deeper cut, and there is great fear about this. And if necessity demands this, you must find an experienced one and with hands, do it where they are found; and if you don't find such a person, you should not hesitate to consult even the subtlest of mirrors.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And there is a small incision in the woman's life, or a woman who knows some part of the art, and she is commanded to do what you command about stone interrogation;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and see very well if that woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she must place her effort or foundation and seek the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she compels her with all her might and seeks the stone, and I advise her to apply all her effort or strength in the area of the body, and presses and urges her left hand against the bladder formation.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she must move it vigorously from the entry of the bladder until underneath, as long as she reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut into the stone at the root of the thigh where it meets the middle of the bone, there where the bones are joined, and feel the bone in that part.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his hands above the stone or nearby; cut him to the first small size.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	Then extend the knife in the cut, if you feel the bone increase the wound as much as the bone can come out forcefully, and know that many types of stones are:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	This is what you should know: there are small and large ones, hard and soft, long and round, and those with bends.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you understand the symptoms to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if he doesn't faint, then put some vitriol powder on him and keep it for an hour until the sweat is completely gone;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work, as long as the stone is strong, and have at hand the instruments I told you about in the extraction of the stone for yourself to help with your task;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if it doesn't hurt you and the artery is severed, if you put the powder on the wound and apply pressure with bandages and bindings, do not repeat this action. Leave the stone alone and don't try to remove it, in case it might kill the patient;
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of blood has calmed down and the limbs have returned to normal, then return to your work, while the stone is still hard.
de hernie carnouse	of fatty hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	A watery ointment is nothing else but a collection of moisture or white fat, which resides in the belly of the animal that contains eggs;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And it is called "fat," and under no circumstances is it properly in the egg's membrane, if one believes that it might be another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	And this is the skin of the neck between the white flesh, as we have said;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And there should not be any lack thereof.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of this mucus is due to weakness that affects the kidneys, and spreads this substance.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And whenever there is percussion on the kidneys, and this moisture has many hues:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it becomes a declining yellow color, or without redness, or black, or aqueous white, and this happens more often;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this assembly; because if it is white flesh as we have said, then it indicates pus that has reached its limit, and lasts as long as an egg's figure, and does not open the kidneys, for it contains moisture throughout.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the actual tissue, then the pus includes part of an egg, and because of this, one thinks it's another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	And if moisture is between the skin of the elbows and the white flesh underneath, you will feel it well;

dou chastrement	Of discipline
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that chastisements and fines are part of our law, and because I prefer not to discuss them in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	And requires for only two ways:

et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	And the other is that we often need to deal with the taming of some animals to help us, such as goats, sheep and deer, and others.

ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either through attraction, or through weakening.

puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then take them with your hand while they recover and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	In the correction of size:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	It is necessary that you dye the beast. Press the skin of its udders with your left hand, then tie the tail ligature, and cauterize each teat individually when you have well scorched them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and I leave no small hole due to scalding and the fine scald that is inside the veins;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	And this method of correction is preferable to that done by attraction because with attraction there might remain some part of the udders, which makes the beast lust for more.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Of Hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermodendry is according to two ways at home:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One way is that between the two udders open just as in the natural figure of a woman, or may have hair, and sometimes through it she urinates.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	The other way occurs among women, with something resembling a penis and two sex organs at the opening.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment of burns and scalds is such that you dress all bandaged areas, treating them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second way, for men whose urine jumps through their foreskins, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	from the cheek area
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A tentigo is a dislocated shoulder in the natural part of the body, until it becomes too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary that you dye away the excess of the tentigo on your hand or nails, and handle it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do not apply too strongly, so that blood does not spill out, then proceed with another treatment until it is clean;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	And there is another condition that emerges from the mouth of the womb, and the thigh, and by chance with a burst of force, and according to its appearance it resembles a cow, and because of this they called it the old 'cow disease'.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If it is necessary that you take care of it, as we have said about the pustule, and the treatment until it heals.
de erratique	Of cautery by fire command to the sickman to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic if either the woman's nature is not fully perceived or the wound is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	And occurs naturally by birth, or through accidents due to illness that has come about;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	Or it's due to a shoulder injury, or from subtle or thick fat, and is performed in the womb, or on the chest, or under the arm, wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	And to conceive, and during childbirth, and by chance one might obtain flowers for having them.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	And the knowledge of these things is by the sight of the body.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	When the stabs are closely apparent, prefer striking at your hands or on the thigh.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it's deep and subtle, and close to the two lungs, hurry up, and do it this way:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Put your two hands together, and have the woman on her back, spread out her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then form both lungs until the subtle syphilitic sore is resolved, and is covered by the remedies;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool and the grease in oil, put it on her body, and have the woman lie at home each day, so that she cannot be cured.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if it is hard and full under the skin, then you must apply a heated spatula resembling a mistletoe leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the remedies are of earthly nature, then suspend them in vinegar and water;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And have remedies for arresting blood loss, such as these, dragon's blood, incense, concoction of abundant egg mixture;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then administer a wide bandage, so that the wound cannot heal over;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and thus for a longer time, and he should have a tent of dry linen;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then perform other treatments as long as it is bleeding.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when it's an injury due to a fall, if you need to treat according to this manner, provided that it's not gangrene.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For the gangrenous abscess in the groin area, one should not use fire to treat it.
des emorroides	Regarding piles (hemorrhoids).
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Emorrhoids are openings of veins that occur without proper care; and when emorrhoids become old they turn into thrombosis.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have mentioned the appearances of these in the section for them, and their symptoms; I will now speak about those that require treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and pus, when they are ripe in the anus, do not appear to touch, except for the cure by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those at the mouth of the anus, which can be felt, are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	So then, you should put the woman in a cool house, place the altar under the knives, and set her on its roots. Then sprinkle powders made from blood-restraining medicines such as acai, dragon's blood, incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then bind his feet to the surface for an hour, then place them in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if there is a bleeding, should it occur, let her sit in a decoction of sumac and the bark of pomegranates and soap and similar things, then take barley flour, mix it with honey and anise, and make a poultice for her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it clots, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, have her undergo suction cups on the back and breasts without causing injury;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take fleece, mix it with the sap of plantain or the sap of agelnier with old wine, and have it applied to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess rests, treat the affected area with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And that which is called "Albathir" is red, and it resembles the head of an asp, if you need to cover it as I have said earlier about the Theulus.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And continue the treatment until sanity is restored.
des apostemes de la marris	The contents of the uterus
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many forms of abscess occur in the marris, such as gangrene and stone-abscesses, herpetic lesions, intestinal ulcers, fistulas, hemorrhoids, and other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	So, I must explain in this treatise the pus-filled wound that comes in the belly, which is not among the abscesses that can be tied off;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you want to understand the working of iron, observe how these pus-filled wounds are red at the beginning of their appearance and filled with heat and fever, and if they turn red, you will be able to see them.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	So don't rush to pierce too soon, but wait until the pain is relieved as much as possible;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	And then have the sick person sit on the chair, and place two small stools beneath where their knees would bend, supporting them with their back and having their feet touch parts in front of the legs.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let her hips be spread apart, and place her arms under her knees, and bind them well with a good band.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then direct her to lean towards the right side, and I will prepare the instrument used for working inside the womb, which comes next.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you see the instrument being prepared, you make your first cut to assess the depth of the womb. So that what enters inside the instrument does not go too deep and cause injury to the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	And if the tools are larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths, so that the tools do not cause discomfort.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	And it is necessary for him to place the tool's cup above and to sharpen the tool.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscesses open and one makes it with a gentle hand, if it suits to cover at the head, at the heart;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	And when the bag is emptied, it is necessary to place in the wound bandages soaked in rose oil, or in dry green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	And place the bandage of the wound at the bottom of the wound, and place it forward on top of the wound and on clean wool that is moistened in water or cooked vinegar;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then after two days of ointment treatment, as long as it is bleeding;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and then each time raise and lift the wound by applying a blister of water and honey, and afterwards with water or roots of lily and aristolochia that have been cooked;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then proceed with the ointment application.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is treated with mustard, you should avoid cooking it with iron, but treat it in the way we've instructed when discussing its application.
de l’enfantement	During childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	The first step in childbirth is for her to recognize the natural birth figure, and you'll notice certain signs when you see a woman preparing to give birth and feeling the urge to push, wanting to smell the air.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	therefore hasten the child to come forth with strength;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	know that this birth is according to the natural figure, and it emerges through her head, and the second stage follows him;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	And when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press his belly, so that the child comes out soon;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when he descends from his head, then comes the second with him, and in this manner she is freed of her excesses by good childbirth management;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	And such other things do not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it comes only on his hands and feet, or under the body or shoulder, or on his belly, or in the groin, and is sometimes transformed by chance around its neck, or through other harmful configurations;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	So skill and subtlety are required in these matters for the midwife, and one must be aware of errors and deception, and I will show you all the forms as to how one should assist them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	When the child comes forth from its head through a natural opening, and the woman gives birth in great pain, and her strength is weak, she should be made to rest on a saddle, or women should hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and from its essence, if fennel has been cooked, then place the baby between her fingers in a small spatula as described here.

si istra maintenant l’enfes.	If you are now taking care of an infant.

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	From the birth of the child above its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes down through its feet, it is his duty to keep them up;

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	from the issue of the child at its knees

de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	from the birth of the child which comes with one hand wide open

adonques si istra legierement.	Therefore, if you gently handle it.
de l’issue des gemelz	from the issues of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that teeth often come out, and sometimes they come out three or four times;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	And this is not an unusual thing, and little happens.

de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	They are not formed in marriage I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or more than fifteen up to XV, and they are all shaped like a child by the measurement of the glorious one's wisdom. It is necessary that the doctor knows all this, for such things might happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	Do it according to what is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	Of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman who has lost her dead child or whose womb is diseased, as I have explained in the division, and if nothing comes out, and you are forced to operate with your hands;

si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary for the woman to be able to stand on her own at the back, and have her shoulders positioned forward, and lift her legs.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And the minister should use two parts of the tincture, or she should be bound to the bed so that she is not moved during childbirth;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of a pregnant woman with moist almond oil using a mixture of rosemary and fenugreek seeds, and linseed. Then anoint her hands with these oils and these mixtures;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then carry her lightly, then when she moves her hips as it is in the instructions, and be careful that when the baby starts descending towards her head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If the gallbladder lodges in its throat or around its neck or in its mouth or on its palate or under the beard or in the armpit or near the ribs, and if it descends into the belly, then it sticks or gets stuck at the mid-ribs;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary for you to cut the gallbladder with your right hand, and place the curvature between his fingers of the left hand, and push it lightly with all his hands, and insert the gallbladder into none of these places that we have mentioned, as long as it does not reach the empty thing;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the gallbladder:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert against another gallbladder, or the third if you need it, so that all extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then extend evenly while moving from one side to the other, for the movement to occur, and whether it's the incisors to keep in place due to movement, as is shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if he leaves out some part of it, if he greases his hands with grease from any of its sides, and rubs them on that part, and pulls the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if there's nothing left of it, place that tooth or higher up in its socket, and do this until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be pulled back by squeezing, then you should wrap around its tendon until it comes out completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then the knife at the joint of the sole or at the cut, and similarly you should do with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is squeezed at the exit, or if its tip has an acutely assembled point, then you should push the sharp thorn of the skull between your fingers, and move the tip and extract the point.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you will find it in the tool which is called "almidach", from this tool comes its form with the tools or chapters that follow this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and similarly, make it so for children with large natural heads;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with tongs, and if the head jumps out and is restrained by force, even if it's broken, until the moisture or pus comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it can't come out, cut it piece by piece as you can manage;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you should pierce him as far as the moisture goes.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, there's a slight pull, and the connection to the mouth of the umbilical cord is also slight.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is swollen in the belly or around the thighs, then you should drain him up to the fold of skin hanging on the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	And stretch the belly or the thighs as far as the moisture that is there;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if any other bones are involved and the head remains, then grasp the socket with your hand from behind until you reach the root of the gum, and pull it up to the mouth of the gum;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then remove the socket or the second bone, and pull it out.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the mouth of the gum is narrowed by an abscess that has come there, then it should not be cut open, rather it should be treated with moist and fatty substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And the surgeon applies plasters, and also uses water that is soothing and moistening.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is under his breast, and you can place it level, then follow what we have said about the live infant;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if one cannot do so, if you pull it by parts, and leave nothing of the tail.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, follow what we have said about treatments for abscesses that come to the gum;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if blood flow stops, then place in water and restraining it, and follow other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman who had borne an offspring that was dead, and then another one on him, and he revived the other.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came in his belly, and it swelled so much that he opened up, and began to have severe pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was summoned for the treatment, and I thought for a long time, and could not accommodate the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I place under a strong attraction, and out comes one bone, and after some days another.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly amazed, for this stomach has no bone.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I want the wound, and when handling bones, until the woman was in her best condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And she tends to keep the woman long enough like this, and it would be a bit of support from the head;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I remember this chapter only because when the masters find a strange thing, they need to know how to provide help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the shoulder back to its place.
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Next comes the description of the presser, which is mentioned in the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and for the second turning of the two shoulders of each hand.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	In every case, the horns should be more delicate than those of the retractor, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let the mouth of the pipe be two palm widths wide, and the margin of the trees must be long, up to one and a half palms;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in between the two levers let there be two attachments of this same pipe, which must be firmly attached on both sides, half a palm long or slightly more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two adjustments are put in the mouth of the mare to open when one turns the second horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, might be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the shape of the pincers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and has two dislocations, as you see, of the length of a palm, and two sticks of width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	And when you see the mare open to all the instrument, have the woman sit on the bed, her knees hanging and her legs spread apart, then place the two adjustments together in the mare, and hold the tip of the instrument under her armpits;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with the whole instrument in the same way as you have done with the pincers equally, according to the amount that you see open the mouth of the mare, as long as the reins do what she desires.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	This tool is entirely mounted, and multiplied according to these similarities;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when you have equipped the tools, then your work becomes faster and more precise, and you stand taller among people due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not hesitate with the instrument until you have arranged it, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second stage is retained during childbirth, it's necessary that you instruct the mother to hold back her waters, and then make her inhale cold air. Afterward, restrain her hands at her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she jumps over it, it's well done.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and make it spill or cover it. Then place herbs that can open the woman's mouth such as mint, rue, anise, chamomile, clove, and lavender;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or any of them, be cooked or boiled on fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then place a stick or a reed in the mouth of the pot, and the other end in the opening of the mortar, and let the steam rise inside the mortar;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If it jumps the second knee quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she still lacks strength after this treatment and has no force, command her to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or musk, and then with the ointment, and wish for a second one;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she has found it, take and extend her gently, so that the mortar does not spill during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But you must gently move it to the right and to the left, and then cut.
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes and becomes dislocated again.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if their nose is blocked by mucus and inflammation, we have said the treatment for sneezing and herb fumigation;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not relieved by all that we have said, be careful not to cut without hesitation;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it should be that the person at the nose opening is tied to the woman's thigh, then she is anointed with ointment and given a suppository treatment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if it does not relieve the pain and will come out forcefully;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but if it does emerge, then when there is a foul smell in the stomach and head, and burns the body.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Then therefore appropriate fumigations must be prepared:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the old ones have experienced the fumigation of watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the tool used to fume the woman during the retention of flowers and the afterbirth is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is like seeing the appearance of a cane, and one places the subtle head in nature, and the shoulders wide on the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And have the fumigations over the coals, and let it cook until it is done, then start another one.
de percier lou fondement	of piercing the base
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but rather it has been disturbed by some subtle cause:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	So then at the birth, let it pierce that cause to its proper place, and do not allow it to be pierced by any sharp tool, and guard the placement so it does not touch;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place on wet wool in wine and oil, then apply the ointment cure until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt it will not resurface, then place or insert a tallow stick and leave it in for several days, and remove it when the child wishes to go indoors.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And here comes this treatment of sudden injuries to wounds or abscesses;
si covient coper celui soudement:	if one needs to cover that suddenly:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	whether it is treated or, as we have said about the opium poppy's root.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula near the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas coming from under the foundation are nodulation, and grow larger those coming from above the foundation or in the space of two parts, if it is one fistula or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that nodulation is old, if it works and brings moist resulting in white or powdery matter, and often these fistulas are painless;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by those who experience or have an emaciation or windiness when the body expels, and sometimes jumps from one to another.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if it's about fistulas that penetrate up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And they reach up to the joint of the knee, and up to the patella.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows whether the fistula is situated at the bottom, and not at all:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And when you press on your index finger or bottom, and you insert a delicate needle like that of an arachnid or iron into the fistula without any twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it is twisted, then you insert a subtle tentacle like that of an octopus, or the hair of a horse, as long as you feel the tentacle or hair on your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you do not feel it, and there is no change in appetite or wind movement or smell, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that she does not pierce through;
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends up to the bladder or up to where urine is conducted, if it causes urination and cannot be sealed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it has pierced up to the knuckle joint, then there is the temptation coming up to the elbow;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no winding and the origin of the pain inside, then it is that it lies within a bone, and it does not benefit from medicine or immediately by salve;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these Persian boils there is no treatment for anything other than work and the vanity of those who interfere with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In those that are neither Persian nor old, there is hope for healing through iron, as I have found out, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And he lifts his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his abdomen;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then bind an araneus tent or a tortoise shell if there is difficulty, as long as you know where the tent comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it in the foundation of their body, then you must press your index finger there, and if it is felt that the tent has been pierced;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And when discovered, or if you feel something between your index finger and the side or the heart, then know that it is deep.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If there's no trouble with it, one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	Nevertheless, one can still often manage to cure some things, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And when assistance is provided, one heats the delicate cautery according to the size of the fistula, as was explained earlier;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and applies it hot into the fistula until it reaches the base;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you know that the burned outchar remnants resemble a bird's feather, which indicates they are fully burnt;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treats the wet areas with butter until the burnt outchar comes out, then applies ointment to cover and join the area.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is so healthy, that's good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	That way, it cannot be healed any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent sticks inside and doesn't penetrate to the root or base, then you place an thick covering of burned outchar or syfac between your finger and the tent, and you see the fistula at the place where the covering meets the skin;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If one begins by applying to the start of the fistula, and holds steady before the tent, then afterwards applies heat after, as long as it reaches the tip of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	And the tent will be released, and there will be no harm.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then remove those veins that seem like a bird's feather, and do not leave any behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the wound doesn't heal, and cuts you instead of flesh, then apply a fire or an ointment to it.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cauteries combine two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	That is to say, the burning of these veins in conjunction, and the removal of blood and the drying out of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then the treatment of wet tents with butter or ground-up herbs, until the limbs are bathed in water, and out comes the burned veins in the water;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with the application of hot compresses made of durable flesh, and apply dried medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, if it heals properly and does not recur.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes just up to the full depth of the wound bed, and is far from the body, you should fill it with your own finger or its depth, and check this.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tentacles, and within II there is silk or yarn or thread, or it is ready to pierce, assuming there is only a path of hope and no other way out, by administering one of these three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have explained, or you cut until the bottom, or if you can find tentacles and apply treatment as first;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and don't cut too close to the foundation, that you might cut through the layer that supports the base, causing forced expulsion of contents by the body;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it, as we have explained;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance if it is healed, or you remove that covering and cleanse it since it has been peeled from the bottom, through trial or with another tool directed.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then purify that pus-filled wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to heal the wound, and to prevent the formation of a窦 in the lower part near the base:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If you can do it more lightly for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And never let ulcers form in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	And when you puncture the ulcer from within, and it is located under the skin near the base, if you take a puncturing tool in this manner:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And attach one and a half twined threads, and insert the tent into the entire length of the thread in the duct until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is deep in the margin near the base inside, then extract that thread of the diseased part, so that when you puncture your tool or the base;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	And stretch the head by pulling the thread, and join together the two ends, binding one to the other, and leave it for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And hold steady once or twice, until the thread covers these marks that are between the two ends, and they stick together;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed and has recovered.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not burst, make it burst in all possible ways that you can, as long as it is not too far apart.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not suitable to sew it up when the wound is too deep and then treat it as we have said, until it heals.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spinous spur that one creates for the fistula is quite small and from both sides, it cuts;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand not, because there's one that should not be cut and one that should not be avoided, as you see here:
des emorroydes	From the arrows.
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Worms can occur in two ways:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	They can be within the foundation, like pieces of resin, and there are small and large ones, bleeding in the center, and there is one or more of them, they lie outside the foundation and at the base of the foundation;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those which are deep if they have little moisture, and even still or a bit of yellow water or a bit of blood, and have the color of the flesh;
