et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And for the treatment of those inside the foundation, you must instruct the patient to secrete through chambers until the foundations release, and it becomes evident that the fibers are present;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, or use pincers to grasp it, or hold it with your nail, then pull it from its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the root cannot hold it due to moisture, take it with its fur, or cloth, or a piece of camel leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And extract them with your hands, then pull, and dust them with some hot powders that are like fire cauterization;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	For you should cauterize them as was said or instructed in the chapter on cautery; then treat other remedies until there is no fever.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the roots cannot emerge, then cauterize the patient using a cauterizing agent that is sharp and rough to wash out what is or has the root, so that it can come out smoothly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patients do not improve and if their hair is thick at the root, then the treatment should be gentle;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And if you take them with your fingernail or tweezers and pluck them out, then treat them as we have said, until there is no fever and they fear the iron cut.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you suture according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a piece of thread, and bind it into a needle. Then stretch the thread upwards and pierce another end of the needle elsewhere. Loop both ends of the thread over the needle and make sure they are wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And tighten the thread in a knot, then cut off the thread, and pull out the needle. Do this process for all others and leave some thread to drain excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the wound a moistened bandage in oil or plaster and put it on the wound. Command the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then let it be until the patient has rested. When they are down, apply ointment treatment and other treatments as long as they recover.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	this means "by drying out or the ground" in modern English. The sentence seems to be part of instructions on how to dry something or set it on a foundation.
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times, there was the drying effect of earth in the intestines, and by the body's natural condition, and when the illness is old and medicine no longer works.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It's necessary that you sharpen to the tip of a spatula or on your nail the skin above, which should not be moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then apply the cure as long as it is firm, just as is necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot become firm, then resume the shave more forcefully than before, until some healing occurs, and may be scorched;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply the cure until it heals.
dou fremit	When the fire cautery instructs the patient to let their hairs grow long and even; if they prick at their base, hold steady until they fully grow.
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A worm is a small rash before the body, and goes throughout;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And when the artery is blocked, it feels cold, and one also feels it like a pulse that has died due to tremors, spreading throughout the body, and more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment involves taking a cane with a goose feather or a strong vulture feather, and placing that stick over the tremors, until the purple circles encompass the entire tremor.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to all of the hair until you grasp it completely by its trembling, and place it downward, and remove the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see this, do as with an arrow or iron in the shape shown, and make it both slender from beneath and piercing above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not neglect, for you must hold with both hands, and gently press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see it, apply the cautery to the trembling, as is shown or detailed in the section on fire cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the bladder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Never use silver, or copper filings, or melted iron or brass;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And never make these small and large instruments according to their users.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when it comes to treating infants and those who are weak and in pain, they need small ones.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the small and large needles is made as follows, or when binding the abdomen according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is an opening or the belly is pierced, as you see, and if the head is inside.
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	And has on one of the sides two missing parts, and on the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let it be in the belly or where we place the medicines of a beast's bladder or parchment, and make all around tiny holes, and have between each hole an inch of space. Then insert into these holes one strong thread of twisted raw silk at either end, and sew the belly up like a goat would;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, if it sticks to the tool with a strong thread in front of it, then proceed with enemas;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And this is the shape of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and smear the area around the anus with oil or yolk of egg, or something similar, then gently apply it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then they guide the eye with both of their hands together until it is fully open, then remove the cataract, and lift the patient's legs to the face, and if the medicine desires to come out, then apply it as much as you can.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if he sleeps through an entire night, that is more assistance.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you administer it during a condition of belly obstruction, and the medicine begins to come out quickly, then continue until it's relieved.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if there's bleeding or at the base or within an abscess, also if there's a cataract so delicate as for an infant;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and it is the form of the delicate cataract on which the skin is constrained:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have spoken about treating wounds in the section on treatment;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we will tell you about treatments for hands and medicine, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are various depending on how they were made, and where they were made on the body, and for what reason they were made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things that lead to wounds are by dint of stone, and the size of a sword or knife, or spear or staff or axe, or similar items;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or according to the body's bones, such as wounds that occur on the neck, or on the head, or in the chest, or the stomach, or the liver, and similar parts;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and begin with wounds on the head that are simple, since the recall will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes or on the head, and if the bone is not broken, take care whether it was caused by stone or similar items, and even though the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, and you slightly doubt an abscess developing.
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	If it is done immediately with the surgeon's knife right away if there is a little blood from the wound and the patient has been treated differently than the excised part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And make the patient drink wine and eat heavy meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if they do not wish to be treated with surgery, then reduce their food intake, and do not drink wine, nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And place on the wound, if we find pus there, wet cotton in oil rose water only, or in wine that is astringent;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no pus present, place on the wound, if it has fresh blood everywhere, and isn't moved by air, powder, that I will mention a little later;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the arm has moved, place some ointments on it, until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like that of a sword cut and similar injuries, and the edges cannot be brought together with stitches, then bring them together by suture, as I will explain for wounds of the abdomen, through sewing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound exposes the bone, it will swell and may only remain for a short while, if treatment is delayed;
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medicine, and replace the hard tissue instead of skin. Instruct the patient to consume fatty meats such as chickens, cooked wheat, like boiled potatoes, and similar items.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find orrotting skin and it doesn't reach the bone, then cut away the rot completely, drain out pus, and then treat.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein without clotting, and it cannot be stopped by medicine, then clip the artery, and if you find it has come loose, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not benefit you, then apply cautery to it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if the wounds are small and simple, their treatment is straightforward:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and then apply this powder which joins together in such a way that when the heat of the fire touches it, it binds firmly.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And here is how to use the powder:
pren encens une partie;	take one part of incense;
sanc de dragon II parties;	add two parts of dragon's blood resin;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	add three parts of fine chalk, and finely ground powder, then fill the wound with it, pressing it firmly until it dries well and binds with all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	and mix it thoroughly, leaving it undisturbed until it doesn't swell;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	For one does not remove the medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And always this is done with the charcoal alone, when one does not have the incense nor the blood of dragon, but when the art has healed the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound has healed within him, even in that state, certainly do not put this powder on it.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some digested poultices, or oat flour mixed with water and honey, until the wound weeps.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then continue other treatments until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if bone fracture comes with the wound and it's small, then use delicate forceps;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about bone fractures in the head later on.
de la plaie dou col	from the wound around the neck.
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This injury occurs in or around the neck; if it is simple, there should be no distinction between this and that around the head, but if a nerve in the neck or an artery has been cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the neck, without any other obstruction, leave the treatment and do not apply anything restrictive, because it harms the neck and causes it to shrink;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not place anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and they are in continuous connection with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	but be it under medicine, as with soap washed in mild water and mixed with rose oil, and lace washed also in mild water, and other earths of the mine in this manner, and wet ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then sew it with bends, until it heals properly.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and the patient is covered with blood, if they puncture or deeper into the body;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if an artery is severed, and blood flows out continually, then to open it, and stabilize, and cautery as needed;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	And if the spinal cord of the throat is severed, or the ears, and guide the passage where the meat goes, so cut the ear above the throat canal, and do not touch the throat but return it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then it tightens the addition, allowing for several days, then treats with dry dressings until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	And if there is an indication of infection in the bone, then one should intervene;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And if there are pieces of bone, if you can remove them all with force, and those that cannot be removed, leave until the wound becomes infected and heals naturally, allowing for its discharge;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I have mentioned on it.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as described in my chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	from the wound of a spear or a knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it's from a spear or a knife, and the wound is deep, examine if there is suction in the wound as long as the patient does not faint:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	Then you will know that the wound is fatal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And if it is not deep, and the wound bleeds freely throughout its length, if one does not apply powder immediately at first hour or bind it up where blood runs freely from the wound and invigorates the heart, leaving the patient in peace.
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	and if you don't have an ointment, put old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture, and let the patient sleep on the wound for three or four days, or longer;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	if there is no spasm, and the heart does not experience harmful tremors or contractions;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see good signs, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat with remedies and other treatments as long as it is clean;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	and if it cannot heal and work, know that there is an abscess;
si la cure si com on doit.	if the treatment should be as it should be.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut, and it's simple or worse, or on the back, then apply the treatment as presented;
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	if it's large, with stitches;
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	and if it's small, with powder; and if it is bruised into the bone, or if there are fragments of bone in it, remove the wound and the external treatments if they have been removed.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they haven't been removed, leave the wound to heal by itself, or facilitate the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other members is the judgement so as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	From the protrusion of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The hernias of the belly are large, medium, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a major wound it can leap out once the intestine or the nerves of the intestines, through which their intrusion occurs;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	And the stitches are more troublesome, and from no wound is it worse than the small one when compared to the large ones; because in this case we cannot set the intestines back into place, unless they are sewn stitch by stitch;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Because the intestines swell as soon as they feel cold; if they cannot be set back into place, then it is better to leave the smaller wound alone, because we must move the intestine back to its original position for others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And know that the rupture of the belly occurs according to four ways:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common incisions happen in the belly seam, and the incision of other wounds on the body has two other seams that are shared with other injuries;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Yet they are more precise with the belly seam, and I will say each one and explain them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small, and no part of the intestine is exposed, and if there's something to be sewn back in place, this is done through one of the two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	Or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it's cold, warm him in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	Moisten an sponge or add a pinch of salt to boiling water only, or cook in boiling water containing cinnamon and pepper and cloves, and stir the intestines until the innards are well cooked.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And once this wine has been strained, and made ready for reducing, it is hot to relieve swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the swelling leave, season the intestines with water or broth and ensure they are fully cooked, because through this method, the entry allows passage for little else;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, make a small incision in the instrument from which one extracts the worms;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	The first treatment is to cook until it reaches the size of the cut, which we should not extend unnecessarily or without significant need;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And these are the tools to open them:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut only within the bend and not outward, and see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged, and the internal organs are displaced, if you can set it back according to its natural form in its proper place, because this counts for movement.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is wide, and it's in the belly area, you should make the patient lie on their back, and place their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	And if it's in the belly area, place their head and bottom higher than other parts. And similarly, if the abdominal rupture is in one of two parts, put yourself such that the injured part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus, it's necessary to follow what I say in large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds, use what you're equipped with; then have at your hands the sacred minister that sears all the injury to its hand and joins the lips.
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	And this is the common method of stitching, and you take one needle or more depending on the width of the wound's size, then leave about half an inch from the edge of the wound, and you put in a needle where there will be enough strong thread;
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	And pierce the two ends of the leather with the two ends of the thorn, which is inside the leather, as long as you make it pierce that part, and join the two ends of the thorn together in four assemblies;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	Then put two strands of doubled thread through the needle from both sides, then join the two ends of the wound together gradually, and then leave about half an inch, and put in another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Then tie the thread like you did with the first needle, and continue doing this according to how many needles you need, until all of the wound is restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	And use needles of medium size, between subtle and bulky ones, because subtle needles cut all the flesh, and the too bulky ones cannot enter well at all.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because it is fitting for them to be of medium size;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	and it is not fitting to have the needles sticking too far out of the flesh and skin, so that they cut and open the wound before stitching;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and when cutting the ends of the needles, ensure they do not irritate the patient while sleeping, and place cloths or bandages around the needle sites to hold them in place, and leave them until the wound has healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	and this method of sewing with needles is more convenient for small wounds, because one or two needles are sufficient.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second stitch is common, it involves joining two shoulder bones and two symphysis bones together on one needle with a strong thread in the middle;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	And when you have pierced all four bones together, remove the needle from where you started, in the manner one sews with thread;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and leave space between each stitch equivalent to the thickness of a small two fingers;
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	These stitches cover the wound, and I sewed a belly cut that someone had made, which was due to a knife cut, and the wound was more than a palm in size, and there were intestines about two palms long, and it was a wound in the middle of the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	I returned his intestine to him once it had been out for twenty-four hours, and the wound was stitched up until fifteen days later. I treated it, and he recovered, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And the priest had judged that he would die, and this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	And I did not treat it with ointment, because I was at sea where none could be found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And I changed the old cotton on it twice a day, and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you two proper methods for suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and make an incision from outside to inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	when it has pierced the center straight in and out, if it touches the scrotum or has caused a wound, then you have made an incision, and make another incision from inside to outside.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And the principle behind this suture is that you sew as the rabbit does with its fur, and you leave one side of the scrotum alone, then take it up again on the other side, until all the suture is completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	The second method of stitching, which Galen described correctly, is such that none do it like this, who join the two parts together naturally, and apply one of the major joints to the other joint in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	Prick an awl or join the major joint to the near one, and only puncture that higher area, leaving the two joints of the same side;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	Then turn the awl and make it pierce from the lower part right up to inside there, of both sides' joints;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both from the lower part right up to inside there, with two more joints of the opposite side that are on the other side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the way of stitching and it is the most common one.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	The surgeon states this sentence, and no one verifies it, thus the abdomen should be sewn with two needles, or where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one should push one needle from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew corroies;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	Know that when the rupture is in the middle of the abdomen, the stitches are more painful than those of their other wounds.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is as follows: just like the judgments for other wounds, it goes like this:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	and it is that when you find the fresh wound filled with all its blood, just as the animal has moved it, then put back the intestine and the cut;
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	Then sprinkle on the powder that stimulates healing, and once it has been applied to the wound, apply no other ointment as long as the wound is open.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and stitch the thread, and let the stitches hold, and let the wound heal;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as others would, until it is clean.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and if you don't have medicines, apply it until the pus starts to drain out. Use old cotton and shake it twice a day until it is clean.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you don't need any other medicines in various preparations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and if you suspect that the wound might cause complications in major body parts, it is necessary for you to soak thin wool in oil of moderate warmth or rosemary oil, and place it between the joints, and over the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	And if there is pain or gangrene in the bowels, and this happens repeatedly, then use black wine enemas, and similarly if the gangrene reaches up to the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce internally, and know that when it's the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the smaller ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	The intestine that is referred to as 'young' cannot heal when it's injured, and this is due to the layout of the veins around it, and the subtlety of the entire body, and its alignment with nerve nature.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if pus jumps out of the wound, reset it as soon as possible like an intestine when it's fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	And if it's old and turned to pus or black, you should tie the black part of the wound, so that no blood flows out anymore, for there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	Then cut the part between the tie and place the two heads hanging from the lower part of the wound until after it is released when pus jumps out, and let the wound heal.
de la routure dou boueil	of the rupture of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	When the intestines are intact, and the wound is small, if it can be restored in some cases, for I have seen that a man was pained or had an abdomen from a lance.
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And it was the wound on the right side of the stomach, and it became stenotic and developed into a fistula, and there was the expulsion and the flatulence.
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied the cure according to what I could, and did not cease refining until it was healed, and the wounds joined.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it heal, I wondered if the patient might be in pain in their stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	And there was no illness, but he remained in better conditions, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And it was said by any experimenter that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be bound in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie, et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les II levres, si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	Take large needles, then bring together the edges of the wound. And when one of the needles has opened its mouth, place it on the two lips if she forces her mouth onto them;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier, puis met I autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	Then press the needle into it, and this stays in place if it can't be pulled out, then put another slight movement after that manner as before, until the wound is entirely filled;
et cout la plaie.	And seal the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide, et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste, en teil maniere:	For these are so intertwined in the intestines, and do no harm to the patient, and one can tie the intestines with a fine thread that has been cut from an animal's intestine, like this:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez, et puis lie au chief de cest fil I fil de lin subtil tort, puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Take the tip of this intestine thread that is quite matted, and then tie it to a thin linen thread you've twisted. Sew it onto the intestine thread with the needle, stitch the intestine, and reset it in the cavity;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitching together ribs is solely based on the path of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is big and wide, especially when it's located in one of the abdominal organs, even if there's no pregnancy or health issue, due to its delicacy.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	regarding a fistula, or if it exists
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	Know that any wound or abscess, as it matures, is universally called "fistula", and even when hair grows there and the swelling recedes.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor, et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	Fistula is according to the hard and white nodule, where no pain can be felt, and it's also feathered like the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes it is clear water, and other times it is thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes little, and other times quite enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char, ce n’est fuers que par une des VIIII causes:	And I have spoken about the classification of wounds in which any wound that is not healed, and there's no flesh, it can only be due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	This means, you need to know about the small amount of blood or pus;
ou por sa malice;	for its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh within it, and above the lips, that does not allow new flesh to form;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or because there is too much wax;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the blood is thickened, and the substance is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine isn't good in the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption is like a pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or due to the property in the area being late for digestion, and slow recovery, escaping naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or because there are veins or bones;
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	And I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments with medicines in this section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	So, it is necessary for me to inform you about the treatment of an abscess which is performed by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas occur in all limbs of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners, ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes, ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	for there are fistulas that come from large veins, and arteries, and nerves, or in the chest, or in the intestine, or in the bladder, or in any of the ribs, or in the spine of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the property of the main body part, and shows its signs.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that occur in this manner are painful to heal, and there is nothing else but treatment, and lack of knowledge;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure, et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And if there is no fistula that does not extend to what I have mentioned, and you undertake the treatment, and understand it well. If you take a spider web or iron wire, if the fistula is straight, then use it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc, car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	And if the fistula is twisted, seek out with a subtle attempt of a thread, for the threads fold and move along the twist.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes, si la clisterize par l’un des pertus, car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	And if the fistula has useless ends and you cannot properly search for it with threads, plug it by one of the useless ends, because moisture will spread from one end to another, then cleanse it.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont, et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	Then feel it carefully with your power, so you know if there is bone or nerve, and feels it completely around, and ask the patient about the pain they feel when pressed by your hand, and find out where he feels it;
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine, ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit, et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	And when you truly know its location, and if it's far from a joint, or nerve, or artery or vein, or in any of the locations I've told you about, do as I have instructed. Remove the bone and the decayed tissues that are inside;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee, et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues, puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule, tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	And then the treatment until it is healed, and if there's a sinus well located in the right place, you should fill it completely with clean pus, as much as possible. Then put wet bandages in medicine for leeches, and leave them up to the tip of the sinus, so that the medicine eats away at the excess that has remained at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then I apply clean bandages until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit, et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if it does not heal through this method, then apply the cautery as we have said, and if the bone is decayed by the sinus, then remove it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	And if the vein or major limbs are involved, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee, puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if the bone is exposed, and there's decay and darkness, then remove it until all decay is removed, then treat with clean flesh until it heals;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant, saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	And if it is not healed, and returns as before, know that you are not quite done until further notice.
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons, et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	If it opens and spreads as long as you're at the bottom, remove all the decay, then return to its proper place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it is well healed, that's fine.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the decay has penetrated too deeply, you cannot reverse it;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	Only due to natural aging if there's no other reason;

Il fut I jovencelz entor XXX ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors, tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	He was a young man around thirty years old, who had pain in his leg due to something that came from within the body, as far as the materials reached the leg, and then there appeared a large abscess, and no external cause existed for opening it.

For during blood evacuation, it often happens, but it was completely healed. In the place of the bone came hard flesh, and it had good consistency with no harm or opposition throughout, neither outside nor inside.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, it should be treated in this manner:

et met I autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os, et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz, et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and put another thread of thicker wool than the first thread, and tie it over the flesh that is inside the bone, and pull such that you draw the decayed flesh away from under it, and expose the flesh on the place where you want to see it, so that it does not hurt the flesh.

si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	If the treatment for the abscess is according to what we have said previously.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	of the abscess under the nail
Panarice est un aposteme que naist desoz l’ungle dou pouchiet de la main, ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	Panarice is an abscess that forms under the nail of the hand's pouch or foot, or by chance forms in other toes;
et quant il est envielliez, et on n’i prent garde, si i vient I aposteme chaus, et corront et giete bowe tant qu’elle corront la racine de l’ungle, et par aventure la corront toute;	And when it becomes old, and if one does not take care, then the abscess may appear, and run and spread as far as the root of the nail, and by chance it might even reach all the way.
et vient li corrosions jusc’a l’os, tant qu’il i vient dolor puant, et est li chiés dou doi larges, et est li color fuxe.	And when corrosion reaches up to the bone, as long as there is piercing pain, and the patient experiences double swelling, and the color changes.
Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu copes a i. fer toute la superfluiteit qui est demoree de l’ungle, puis cauterize la plaie aprés.	When you treat it as we have instructed in the division, and if the treatment doesn't help, then you should proceed to clip all the excess that has remained from the nail. After that, cauterize the wound.
Li cauteres est mout grans aide se li os est sains, et li ungle est sainne;	The cautery is very effective when the bone is healthy, and the nail is healthy;
et se li ungle apresse la char ens, et l’encomence a poindre, et la blece, si covient que tu mettes lou rait desoz l’ungle que point la char, et la boute en haut, et cope celi char subtilment et legierement, et met sus le remenant de la char medicines ardans et corrosives por oster tout;	And if the nail gets infected with pus and begins to swell, causing pain, it is necessary that you place a hot rod near the nail so that the pus points outwards, then lift it upwards, and remove this thin and gently the pus. And place on top of the pus medicine that is hot and corrosive to remove everything;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the treatment of ointments until it is healed.
Et se li corrosion est en l’os, si le cope, et trai fuer, car tant com li os corrumpus i est, si ne puet saner;	And if the corrosion is in the bone, you must remove it and dig deeply, for as much of the bone that is corrupted cannot heal;
et se tu vois le doi corrumpre, si le cope en I des nous si com il est devant dit, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you see the knee corrupted, remove it from us as was said before, then treat it until it is healed;
et s’il est ferus, et boutez, et il sent grant dolor, si covient que tu le sainnes premier;	And if it's hardened and pained, with great pain being felt, it is necessary to heal it first;
puis cope l’ungle dou spatumile agut en taillant de travers desus, et warde que li taille ne viegne jusc’a la char qui est desoz l’ungle, car li malaides sentiroit trop grant dolor;	Then trim the nail under the spatumil at an angle from above, and be careful that the cut does not extend to the flesh beneath the nail, for it would cause too much pain;
et s’il avient, si met chose sus qui apaise.	And if this happens, put something on it that soothes.
la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	The pain originated from the hand
Li dois ajostez qui naist en mains d’aucuns homes par aventure est toz charnus, et par aventure i a teil ou il a osses, et aucune fois i a ungle, et aucun d’aus naissent en la racine de la jointure, ou li naissance est en aucuns nous des dois.	I must adjust what is born in the hands of some men by chance and are very muscular, and by chance there may be bones here or there where they have bones, and none of them has a nail, and no one of these are born at the root of the joint, or where birth occurs in any way.
Cil qui naist en aucune nout dou doi ne se muet, et cil qui naist a la jointure dou doi, par aventure se muet;	Those born in no new note do not move, and those born at the joint of the old bone, by chance do move;
la taille de celui qui est charnus si est legiere, en teil maniere:	The size of the one who is muscular is so light, in such manner:
taille le en sa racine d’un large spatumile.	Cut it at its root as wide as a thumb.
Cil qui naist en la racine de la jointure si est grief a curer:	Those that are born at the root of the joint require cure:
si te tien dou coper.	if you hold it with copper.
En celui qui naist ou doit au derrien nout, si covient que tu copes premier la char reondement jusc’a l’os, puis cope l’os a une soie convenable a ceu, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	In the one who is born or should have at the end of the bone, it's necessary that you first cut up to the soft tissue until the bone, then cut the bone with a suitable tool for this. Then treat it as long as it remains sound.
Li soudemens que vient as dois ensamble vient par naissance, ou par soudement de plaie, ou par arsure de feu, ou par semblans choses.	The fusions that occur at the joints are due to birth, or by the welding of wounds, or by the action of fire, or by similar things.
Si couvient que tu copes celle soudeure, si que li doit repairent selonc lor formes naturelz;	If it is necessary that you work that weld, so that it should be repaired according to its natural forms;
puis met entre dous tentes ou drapelz moilliez en oile roset, qu’il ne se soudent;	Then place between two wet tents or cloths soaked in rose oil, so that they do not fuse;
ou tu met entre dous pieces de plonc subtilz, tant que li leus soit soudez, si com il covient.	Or you put between two delicate pieces of leather, until their welding is done, as it should be.
Se soudemens vient a aucun de ses dois avec la paume, si cope celle sodure si com il covient.	Welding occurs at none of his joints with the palm, if you take care of this welding just like it should be.
des vils	Of low-quality
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	The veins are thick, rolled-up, full of excess melancholic substances, which come from the head of many members.
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	And more occurs in legs of those who walk on foot and work and carry, than in others.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	It follows therefore that you must administer one time a bloodletting procedure, and then heal it using basilica.
Li cure de fer si est selonc II manieres:	The iron treatment is according to two methods:
l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	One method is that you apply them, and drain the black blood;
et li autre maniere si est que tu lieves la voinne, et la trai toute fuer.	And the other method is that you open the vein, and drain it all forcefully.
Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere:	The cut is according to this method:
arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez, puis estrain la jambe dou malaide des desus la cuixe jusc’a la partie desoz le genoil;	First, immerse the leg in hot water for a while until the large veins are thin. Then stretch the leg from below the knee up to the part above the knee.
puis cope la voinne en I leu, ou en II ou en III, d’une taille large, puis eslieve et trair fuer le sanc noir a ta main, des l’un chief jusc’a l’autre, tant que tant de sans en isse com li vertus dou malaide puet soffrir;	Then open in my left or right side, from one large area, then lift and pull strongly for the black blood with your hand, from one side to another, as long as you are able to extract much blood that the virtues of the diseased body can bear;
et puis la lie, et li comande qu’il se teigne de viandes enjanrant cole noire;	and then rub it, and instruct to dye with black meat juice.
et recomence l’evacuation et la sainie quant les voinnes sont plainnes, et nuist au malaide.	And repeat the evacuation and cleaning when veins are full, causing harm to the diseased person.
Li alevemens de li est selonc ceste maniere:	The method of treatment is as follows:
reis la jambe dou malaide, s’il i a mout de poil, puis le met ou bain, et li arose la jambe d’aigue chaude tant qu’elle deviegne rouge, et enflent les voinnes;	Lift the diseased leg, if there is much hair, then dip it in hot water, and lift the leg in hot water until it turns red and veins swell.
et se tu n’as point de baing, si le chaufe au feu, et puis le cope endroit la voinne dou lonc au chief dou genoil, ou en la partie desoz a la cheville;	And if you do not have a cautery tool, heat it with fire, and then apply it to the vein along its entire length from the neck down to the knee, or in the part below to the ankle.
puis aoevre le cuir a l’oncine, et escorche la voinne de chescune part, tant qu’ele apere quant on la sent;	Then cut the skin with an awl, and scorch the vein from each side, until it appears when one feels it;
et on la voit rouge et noire, et quant elle entre ou cuir si semble ausi com une corde blainche;	And you see it red and black, and when it enters or appears as if a white string under the skin;
puis boute le rait desoz, tant qu’ele soit alevee dou cuir, et puis la pent a l’oncine legier, puis le cope en I autre leu ensus III dois;	Then pull the vein outwards until it is raised from the skin, and then cut with an awl gently, then apply it to another area above three fingers;
puis escorche le cuir sus la voinne tant qu’ele apere, puis la lieve au rais, si com tu as fait, et la pent a un autre uncine, si com tu as fait premiers;	Then scorch the skin above the vein until it appears, then gently pull with the thumb, just as you did, and cut with another awl, just as you did first.
puis cope une autre taille, ou plusors se tu en as mestier, puis la lieve, et la cope au doi dou piet, puis la trai et lieve jusc’a la seconde taille;	Then take another size or more if needed, then lift it, and hold at the knee of the foot, then guide and lift until the second size.
puis l’estrai de taille en taille, tant qu’elle isse toute fuer, puis la cope;	Then strain from one size to another, until all the strength has come out, then take it.
et se tu ne la pues traire et lever, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil fort double, et la lie et la trai, et i boute desoz I rait, et torne ta main d’une part et d’autre, tant qu’il en isse;	And if you cannot strain and lift it, use a needle with all the strong thread doubled, tie it and guide it, then cut on both sides, and turn your hand from side to side, until it passes through.
et garde qu’elle ne cope, car s’elle cope, si ne la puet on traire ne lever, et en vient nuisement au malaide;	And make sure it doesn't stick, for if it sticks, one cannot strain or lift it, and this causes harm to the patient.
et quant tu l’as toute traite, si met sor le leu de la plaie laine moillie en vin et en oile roset;	And when you have strained it completely, place wet wool in the wound soaked with wine and rose oil.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the treatment as long as it remains clean.
Et se li vis est contraite et torte et envoloupee ensamble, et ele n’est mie droite, si com nos avons dit, si covient que tu la fendes tortement, mais ne la coper mie;	And if the limb is twisted and turned all together, and it is not straight, as we have said, then you must cut it in a twisting manner, but do not sever it;
et la trai si com nos avons devant dit.	And guide it as we have explained before.
Li forme dou fer dont on cope la vis si est corbes, et ne trenche mie, qu’il ne cope la voinne;	The shape of the iron with which you twist the screw is curved, and does not cut, so it does not sever the vein;
et est de grosse corbeure, car s’il estoit subtilz, si coperoit la voine, mais soit gros si com nos avons dit, et ci est li forme:	And it has large curves; for if it were thin, it would cut the vein, but be thick as we have said, and this is its shape:
de la voinne civile	of the civil vein
Ceste voinne est enjanree en jambes, en chaudes parties ou il ne naist herbes ne arbre, et en terre ou il n’a point de moistor;	This vein runs through legs, in warm areas where no herbs or trees grow, and in soil that lacks moisture;
et par aventure naist autre part qu’en jambes, et ceu avient de la porriture que vient desoz le cuir, si com il vient dedens le cors serpens et vers, enjanrez entre cuir et char.	And by chance it is born in another place than the legs, and this happens due to disease that comes from under the skin, as when it occurs inside the body like snakes and worms, squirming between the skin and flesh.
Et se li signes de l’encomencement de ceste voinne si est qu’il vient en la jambe une tres grans enflammation, puis se chainge li leus, et comence li voinne fors issir, ausi com une racine d’une plante.	And if the signs of this vein's beginning occur such that there is a very great inflammation in the leg, then the veins change, and the vein starts to emerge outside, like the root of a plant.
Quant li chiés apert, si covient que tu envoloupes entor une piece de plonc des une З et demi jusc’a II З., et la noe, et laisse le plonc pendant a la jambe, et totes les fois qu’il en ist point au defuer, si l’envoloupe entor le plonc, et la nowe;	When the shoulder is separated, it is necessary that you wrap around it with a piece of oak about one and a half times up to two times., and tie it, and leave the oak on the leg, and every time there's need for more, if you wrap around the oak again, and tie.
et s’elle est trop longe, si en cope une partie, et envoloupe le remenant, et ne la coper mie en sa racine, tant qu’elle soit toute issue;	And if it's too long, if you cut off a part and wrap the remaining back around, and don't overlap in its root, until all is out.
car se tu la copes, si rentre en la char, et fait venir aposteme et porriture ou leu, et male maladie;	because if you overlap it, if it enters the flesh, and brings abscesses and disease or injury to its place, and causes bad illness;
por la queil chose il covient qu’elle soit traite poc et poc jusc’a chief, et n’en remaigne rien ou cors;	Because of this matter it is necessary that she be treated slowly and gradually until completion, and does not leave any remainder or excess;
et est aucune fois ceste voinne quant elle est traite de V paumes de lonc, ou de X, et uns hons vint ja a moi, a cui elle issit de X paumes de long, et quant tu la copes, si boute I rais ou pertus, et la perce jusc’a fons, si que tout en isse;	And in each case when she is treated for so many palms or X, and a short period of time has passed since she was X palms long, and only recently did she reach that length, after it was treated. If you take her pulse now, if there are one or two beats left over or missing, and you puncture until the bottom, ensuring everything comes out;
et soit vuidie li matiere qui est dedens, et amenistre au leu medicines enjanrans porriture aucun jor, puis le cure si com les apostemes.	And empty the substance that is inside, and administer to the limb remedies for pus every day, then treat it like abscesses.
Et aucune fois a ceste voinne mains rains, et meismement quant elle apert en la jointure dou piet, ou ou piet, et i vient mout de pertus, et dont il saut rains;	And always for this vein in the hand, and similarly when it opens at the ankle or knee joint, and there is much missing pulse, and where it remains;
cure le donques si com nos avons dit devant.	Cure it then as we have said before.
des vers qui naissent entre cuir et char	worms that come to life between skin and flesh
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «maladie de buef», por ceu qu’elle avient maintes fois as bués, et est un petis vers qui naist entre cuir et char, et va par tout le cors montant et dessendant, et le sent om bien a l’aler de membre en membre, tant qu’il desront le cuir ou il vait, et saut fuer;	This disease is called in our land "cow disease," because it happens to cows many times, and it is a small worm that is born between the skin and flesh, and travels throughout the body, going up and down. It makes one feel ill from member to member, until it leaves the skin where it was heading, and jumps out forceably;
et est enjanrez de porriture d’aucunes humors, si com vienent vers et serpens et lumbris et ascarides ou ventre;	and it is filled with corruption of some bodily fluids, such as oozing, serpents, worms and roundworms in the stomach;
et doute on de son malice, car quant il va par le cors, et il monte au chief, et il vient a l’oil, par aventure rentre, et destruit l’oil;	And there is doubt about its nature, for when it travels through the body, and goes up to the head, and reaches the eye, by chance it returns, destroys the eye;
et ceu avient maintes fois.	This happens many times.
Quant tu le vues curer et traire, si ne puet on fuers que quant il vait:	When you see it being treated and bled, if one cannot remove it until it is about to:
si covient donques que tu lies le leu desus et desoz d’un fort liien bien estroitement, puis cope sus et le trai fuer, et se li vers est em parfont en la char, et tu ne le trueves, si le cauterize de feu sus, tant qu’il muire;	So then, you must bind the leg above and below with a strong, tightly-wound rope, then cut upwards and bleed it, and if it is located in the flesh, and you don't find it, then burn it with fire while bleeding until it dies;
et li plus grans nuisemens que il fait, si est qu’il corront l’oil, si com nos avons dit;	And the greatest harms that it causes, if run to the eye, as we have said;
et se tu le vois venir ou chief pres de l’oil, si estraint desoz lui le sorcil forment, puis cope sus, et le trai fuer;	And if you see it coming close to the eye, then bind closely around it, then cut upwards and bleed it;
et covient user le malaide de mundifiement de cors de medicines solutives por les males humors porries, et se warse de viandes enjanrans porriture.	And it is necessary to use the remedy of purification for body ailments caused by bad humours, and to be wary of meat causing putrefaction.
de la dolor qui vient de ventositeit	The pain comes from winds or windiness.
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «vakirir», et est une dolor que vient en aucuns membres, et pues se mue de membre en membre;	This disease is called in our land " vakirir ", and it is a pain that comes to any limbs, and then spreads from one limb to another;
et je vis ceu que je vos di.	and I see what I am telling you.
Je fui apelez a une femme malaide, et me descovrit som bras, et vis une petite enfleure en la voinne dou brais;	I was summoned to attend a diseased woman, and she showed me her arms, and I saw a small swelling in the vein under the arm;
et I poc aprés, li vis monter ausi com un ver a l’espaule, plus tost que nulle chose, ausi com vif argent quant il cort de leu a autre;	and after that, I saw it rise as if it were a worm on the shoulder, quicker than anything else, like quick silver when cut from one place to another;
li dolor se departit de celui leu, et se ficha en l’espaule, et puis un poc aprés corrut par tout le cors, tant qu’ele vint en l’autre brais;	the pain left that side and stuck into the shoulder, and soon afterwards spread throughout the body, until it reached the other arm;
puis me contait qu’elle tornioit adés entor le cors, si com je la vis.	then she told me that it was tearing through her entire body, just as I saw it.
Je me mervillai mout coment elle se movoit ensi de membre em membre, car je n’avoie onques veut ceste maladie selonc ceste maniere.	I marveled greatly how she moved from limb to limb in this manner, for I had never seen such an illness conducted like this before.
Toutevoie, je avoie veut maint que bien avoient veut movoir dolor de leu a autre, mais je ne l’avoie mie veut, si com je le vis en la femme;	In every way, I wanted many to want to move the pain of another, but I never did want it, just as I see in women;
et je me pensai que c’estoit por ceu que li femme avoit sec cors, et les voinnes descovertes, et por ceu apparoit celle ventositez constrainte;	And I thought that was because women had smooth skin, and their veins exposed, and that shows the constriction of wind;
et n’aperent mie selonc ceste raison a ces qui sont delicious, et qui ont moistes cors et voinnes reponues.	And they do not see this according to that reason among those who have smooth skin and their veins covered.
Et quant tu vues curer ceste maladie, et li malaides sent celle dolor, s’elle t’apert si com nos avons dit, si la lie desus et desoz hastanment, et puis cope sus tant que cele ventositez constrainte au leu isse fuer;	And when you see to cure this disease, and the patient feels pain, if it opens up like we said, open it quickly from top to bottom, and then proceed as long as that constriction of wind within the body subsides;
et cauterize le leu;	And apply the cautery to the area;
et se tu ne la vois a tes eulz, si le cure de ceu qui deboute les ventositez, si com pilules fetides, et pilules de serapin, et semblans autres.	And if you do not see it at your eyes, when curing the one who dislocates winds, such as foul pills and serpent pills, and similar others.
des saiettes	Of arrows
Les saiettes sont diverses, selonc lor semblances et selonc les leus dou cors ou elles chient.	Arrows are diverse, depending on their appearances and the locations where they pierce the body.
Li diversitez de lor si est qu’il i a de celles qui ont grans pointes, et petites, et chevees, et soudees;	The variety of these things is that there are those with large spikes, and small ones, and those that are pointed, and those that are glued;
et de celles qui ont II angles, et de celz qui ont lengues, et de celles ou il a pieces;	And of those that have two points, and of those that have tongues, and of those that have fragments;
et celle qui chiet en aucun membre si chiet selonc II manieres:	And there's the one that leaks from no body part but leaks in two ways:
ou en membre principeil cheveit, si com cerveil, cuer, foie, pormon, rains, intestine, vessie, et semblans membres.	or from the main body parts where it leaks internally, such as the brain, heart, liver, stomach, kidneys, intestines, bladder, and similar organs.
Quant elle chiet donques en aucun leu de ces membres, et li signe de mort, que je te dirai ci aprés, t’aperent:	When then it leaks not from any part of these limbs, and the sign of death that I will tell you later becomes evident:
si covient que tu te warses de l’estraction de ceste saiette, car li mors vient aprés en plusors dispositions;	If it is necessary for you to take out this arrow, because death comes after in various arrangements.
et quant cist mal signe ne t’aperent mie, et li saiette n’est mie em parfont, si la trai, et cure la plaie.	And when that bad sign does not appear and the arrow is not fully out, you should extract it, and treat the wound.
Et li signe dou cerveil quant li saiette i chiet et perce l’os, et saut li syfac fuer qui est sus le cerveil, est quant scotomie et sode et esvertin et roujor ens eulz, et enflammation et roujor de lengue, et spasme et permixtion d’entendement, et vomissemens de cole;	And the sign of the brain when the arrow passes through and pierces the bone, and blood spurts out where it touches the brain, is when paralysis and numbness and vertigo occur, and a red tongue, inflammation and redness on the skin, and muscle spasms, confusion in thinking, and vomiting of bile;
et per aventure ist sans fuer des narines, ou des oreilles;	And perhaps it affects the strength of the nostrils, or of the ears;
et par aventure pert la parole et la voix;	And sometimes it affects speech and voice;
et saut de la plaie moistor blanche semblant a poulz, et en saut ausi com bruee de char;	And from the moist wound, white pus resembling hair appears, and also in that jump like charcoal ash;
et se cist signe t’aperent, si te tien de la cure, et trai la saiette s’elle n’est ens.	And when you notice this sign, take care of the treatment, and pull out the arrow if it is there.
Li signe de la siette quant elle chiet ou cuer, sont qu’elle est pres de la mamele senestre, et sent ausi com s’elle estoit fichie en chose dure, ne mie vuide;	The sign of the arrow when it bleeds or stings, is that it's close to the left mammary gland, and also feels as if it's stuck in something hard, not empty;
et par aventure li siette se muet ausi com li poulz, et en cort noir sanc, et vient froidor et suor froide, et sincope:	And by chance the arrow also stops bleeding like hair, and black blood comes out, and coldness or cold sweat appears, and fainting:
saiches adonc sens doute ke li mors dessent.	So, without doubt, know that the person will die.
Et li signe de la saiette que nevre lou pormon est que sans plains d’escume saut de la plaie, et li gorge enfle, et li malaides mue color, et sospire haut et quiert le froit ar.	And the sign of an arrow that never leaves its wound is that without any foam spilling from the wound, and the throat swells up, and the patient's face turns a different color, and they sigh loudly with cold chills.
Et se li saiette chiet en la coverture dou pis, si est delez les petites costes;	And if the arrow bleeds in the undercoat near the buttocks, it is deep within the smaller ribs;
et giete grant alainne et grant dolor et sospire;	And causes great pain and great suffering and sighing;
et li muevent tuit li membre des espaules.	And it moves the entire limb from the shoulders.
Et se li saiette chiet ou stomac, par aventure si saut de la plaie aucune chose de la viande indigeste.	And if the arrow stops in the stomach or intestine, by chance if it breaks out of the wound, there's no undigested flesh.
Et se li saiette chiet ou ventre, et en saut point de fien par l’intestine rout, si n’a point d’esperance en la cure, ne en l’estraction de la saiette.	And if the arrow stops in the belly or abdomen, and it jumps out of the wound not through the intestines, there's no hope for treatment, nor is there any hope for extracting the arrow.
Et se li saiette chiet en la vessie, et li urine en saut et vient defuer, et li malaides sent fort dolor:	And if an arrow lodges in the bladder, and the urine escapes in jumps and leaks out, and the patient feels intense pain:
saiches que li plaie est mortelz.	Know that the wound is fatal.
Li autre membre, si com li faice et li colz et li gorge et li espaule et li adjutoire et li espinee dou dos et li forcele et li cuixe et les jambes, et li membre semblant, sont sauf selonc plusors dispositions.
