et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	And then the stretching of a long strip, and if the earlobe is well formed as large as the width of the hand, and it stretches, just like it should.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the breakage is at the front, it is necessary to place an electrode above and another under in the sole of the foot, so that the hand be open and straight, then tie it completely around the hand, and seal the connection between the fingers.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the disconnector comes to break any of our toes, it's like it's twisted, so put them equal, just as it should be;

et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	And if the disconnection is at other toes, like in the index or one of the others, put them equal, and hold it with the healthy toe that follows;
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	Or tie them all together in an 'I' shape, if it moves, or place them on an earlobe, as one would wrap.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	And take care in the restoration and arrangement of each abscess, and aid those who come with it, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	Of the broken kneecap
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The bones of the elbow are often broken, and well can be seen when it turns both forward and backward;

et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	And hold it so that it doesn't move from its place, then leave him like this. Then wait until no abscess forms or there's any other sign.

de la ruelle dou genoil	from the garden alley

de la brisure des os dou piet	From the breaking of bones at the knee

de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	of the breaking of the hand bone

dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	Of the member which becomes weak after garrisoning
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the breaking of the bone is restored, and after that the limbs remain weak and delicate, it happens through various reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	Of which one is due to the fact that it was tied too tightly, and wasn't allowed to be tied as it should have been;

et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and restores its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	If the member is bent after illness
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and if a bone is broken open, even though the form of the limb may be ugly, it still retains its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	do not believe the fools who say that we should break the limb completely anew, and many people have done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	such practices are criticized, causing great harm, and even death in some cases;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	Nevertheless, if the blisters and pains are fresh, it is good to immerse them in hot water, or to cook soothing herbs, such as leaves of savory, roots, and borage, and similar things;
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and make them apply a soothing paste, such as well-made yarrow, and you take the savory muscle extract, and cook it with fat of geese or oil of saffron, and make an application with;
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	or you take dried figs and mix them with hog's tallow, and similar medications that reduce the burning.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And never is removed the operation of rubbing constantly and for a long time with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And let there be a movement to the member every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the stiffness has aged and hardened like bone, and requires roasting with iron, then it's appropriate to cut until you reach the bone, making a subtle incision lightly.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	And apply diligence and study in the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	This begins the book on dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing great pain and injury to the patient.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation affects any part, if the situation requires it now, you should attempt to reduce or reset it without delay.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if one delays, the limbs will swell, and by chance they might be put back into joint pain in the limb;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	By heavens, it should not be moved when it is swollen at that hour:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	Many times it brings on pain and other sufferings;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	Nonetheless, when this happens, have the surgeon care for the patient, then leave him alone until all abscesses are at peace;
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then immerse the limb in hot water and oil, then gently reset it, and treat each member as their treatment comes to its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have arranged the chapters on shoulder dislocations up until this point.
des mandibules	of the jaw
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	It happens that the jaws are dislocated downwards, and the dislocations of both shoulders follow two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	They are somewhat hardened at their ends, and slightly softened.
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	They are completely dislocated and hanging towards the buttocks, and can't hold their saliva in, nor can they close their mouth; instead, their tongue is enveloped by speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it can return through various positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it's whole and complete, you must reset it quickly without hesitation;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	And in such a way that the ministers cut on the head with the aid of someone else, and push one of their thumbs into the socket of the malaide at the root of the mandible's dislocation inside the mouth; if the dislocation is from two parts.
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	And the other should have their hands forward for making it even.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	And instruct the patient to soften them, their jaws, and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And keep the fingers steady until they return to their place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if it returns with pain, even if the two jaws are together, if they are immersed in hot water and oil, as long as you gently manipulate them;
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Do not be afraid to return it, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are returned equally, and the mouth of the patient closes well upon softening, then place them on wet cloths in a poultice made of oil roset and beeswax, then bind them gently with moist linen;
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	And let the patient rest on his back, and the head stays between two cushions, so that he does not move nor to the right nor to the left, nor forces himself to twist, but should only eat light meat until the pains subside, and tie the jaws.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then, gently taste it, and doesn't cause any trouble in opening the mouth for eating and drinking, until the jaw is well set and healed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two lower jaws cannot be properly aligned within an hour and are not turned back to their original position, fever and chronic fatigue will result, and in some cases, abdominal pain or vomiting will occur.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see that, then know it's destruction;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	And often, the one who has this will die within nine days.
de la forcelle	from the lever (referring to mechanics or possibly medical tools)
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The forces cannot displace from within along the middle of the chest and the back; it is displaced only outward, and one feels this clearly.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And for its restoration, let the wounds lie supine on their back and extend their arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	And then press it with your palm in its original shape, and it will return to normal;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	Then place it on the plaster and cover it with a bandage, and secure it;
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	And the shoulder opposite the knife cannot dislocate;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	If it doesn't move, and if it dislocates once, then reset it to its place, as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then place it on the plaster and the bandage, bind it, and instruct the patient to rest until they are sound.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And in this way, the shoulder blade is brought back when it has been displaced from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	On the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Know that the shoulder only dislocates in three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	The first way is when it dislocates from the part of the scapula to downward;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	And the second is at the bottom part;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	And by chance dislocates from the top part, and this happens rarely;
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	And does not dislocate behind for the shoulder, and does not dislocate within for the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	And many times dislocates away towards the elbow, even in those with little flesh, for in these cases it moves quickly;
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	In those who have enough flesh, it jumps to the bone and returns to the bone.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	By chance, it happens to some men from a blow or dislocation, and the shoulder swells with an abscess filled with heat, and they think that she is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	So you must verify it, as long as you are certain;
et adonques encomence la cure.	And then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And you will recognize dislocations when it moves towards the elbow, and you can make a distinction between the diseased shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find the obvious diversity between them;
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	And you will find a hollow at the top of the shoulder, and along the elbow to the neck, as if it were an empty space;
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	And the patient cannot bring their hand to their nose, nor move it with any movements;
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	And also, if it is dislocated high up, if it's not hidden, because you clearly find it at the temple;
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	This way of dislocation can only be corrected when new, or when the child is still small.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the method is for the doctors to lift the hand from the child's head at first, then place their palms under the armpit, and lift the joint up forcefully towards the shoulder.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	And the doctors lift the hand and extend it upwards before placing it under.
si venra hastanment.	If it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it doesn't come as we have said in the following days, then you should immerse the patient in hot water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	And the healer gently relaxes and soothes it, as with an infusion of rosemary, fenugreek, and melilot in water, and it should be prepared.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	Then sew the wounds on his back, and place a piece of soft, even wool under his armpit, not too soft nor too hard. Then position one's heel on top of the wool, and lift the shoulder blade with a strong yet gentle movement, and pull the hand towards the discomfort.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	And assist in lifting the back of the affected limb, so that it does not move downwards;
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	This shoulder is returning now, and if you see whether to reset it according to this manner:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	And be sure that what you prepare at home is larger than the discomfort;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	And keep it straight towards the chest, and support the shoulder under the ribcage of the patient, lift the ribcage upwards, so that the patient hangs down.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	And have another assistant guide your hand from behind towards the abdomen.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the body is too light, it can carry nothing heavy, and the dislocation returns immediately.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And you can also perform this reset in other ways:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	and place it like a long spike in the ground, so that the shoulder is also held upright like a pistol, and not too large or too loose;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then place it under the patient, but make sure there is soil underneath, and the patient stays upright for the length of the staff;
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	then extend her hand downwards on the other side, and the joint will return to its place quickly;
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	And if she does not wish to return due to all these things we have said, then perform this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	Take two large sticks from the shoulders and four broad ones, which have their heads rounded so they can enter smoothly into the socket, following this shape:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	Then fasten at the head of the pole covered with cloth so it doesn't irritate the skin, then place it next to the socket according to the patient's skin;
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	Stretch your arms on the pole from the top and fasten the aid to the pole, and put your arm at the head of the hand. Then place the arm onto one of a long stick about broad, making sure both hands are facing down. Leave the body hanging on the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint now begins to return.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when she is in this condition, no matter how it may be, if you need to place a piece of equal thread over the joint, then apply plaster mixed with flour from the mill, along with incense and egg yolk oil over the entire shoulder and around it, then remove the thread when done applying, and tie the bandage over the plaster, and wrap your hand around her neck, and keep your hands in this position.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And it is necessary for him to move slightly, as long as the limb is stabilized, because he will heal more quickly;
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then move more after five or seven days, and start exercising;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	and if it is hard and not softened, you will find it healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is out of place due to moisture that has come or for some other reason, it is necessary that you apply three cauterizations to it, as was mentioned in the section on cauterization.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all of this, and it dislocates after seven days, and the joint doesn't hold, and can't lift their arm up, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is either cut, stretched or softened;
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and you will know that the joint will never settle in its place again.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation near the buttocks and breasts, or behind, if it is caused by pushing and stretching of hands, is administered elsewhere;
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat until it becomes clean.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing there are still pains in the member and late movements, then one should bathe their body many times, until those pains ease away, and it returns to its original condition.
de la dislocation dou coute	From the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the shoulder joint is dislocated at its tips, and comes back to them;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And it is dislocated in all directions, as well as in front and behind. The dislocation is not corrected because one can see it clearly and feel it distinctly;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	And dislocates according to each form.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you unite the knife with your hand, if you can see it clearly open.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is sore, and cannot bend the arm or reach his shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And you should reset it this way that abscesses are both placed and move away, for if they were placed and came in, it would be a complaint to bring them back;
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	And by chance cannot be reset completely all at once, even when it's behind;
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	It is worse than other dislocations and causes more pain, and by chance death comes to it.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And this restoration is, when it's like this that one can bring back, you extend his hand to your two hands;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And his arms are spread out, and the hands direct towards the center of the elbow both inside and outside, forwards and backwards. Force the joint back to its position either at the top of his shoulder or at the base of his palm, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And when the dislocation is forward, it returns whenever it doubles its hand with its own and pushes from the base of the palm using the lever that is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to return to place, administer strong stretching;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	And when you have administered the extension, both hands hold the arm and apply it firmly, so that it does not move during stretching;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	Then turn the arm from every side, then that you have enveloped a double flag long and wide;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	And when the eye touches the joint with its hand, if it rubs with any oil to soften the joint, then shape the joint properly, until it heals;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	And when it's in place, she places a dry plaster with egg white on it and holds it steady. Shape the area, and allow the arm to be bent at the neck of the patient, then leave it for some days. Afterwards, release it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firm in its place, remove the bandage and leave it;
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	And if you notice that the joint is not healing properly, redo the plaster and the bandage, then leave it like this for a few days until it's firmly in place;
puis le deslie.	Then remove the bandage.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if they feel pain after returning the joint, and it moves again, then wash and scrub beautifully, press until the discomfort is relieved;
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	or you place a thick layer of fatty lamb fat on the joint, then leave it for a day and a night, then apply heat, and let him take a bath;
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	and when it sweats, gently rub the joint, then put the fat back on, and then take a bath;
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this two or three times, until it is healed;
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	and if you see that, put moist cow dung heated with butter on it, and apply heat;
si revenra a sa disposition.	if it returns to its place.
li dislocation de la main	The dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The wrist dislocates and its return is light, more than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	In all cases, it is advisable to return it to its normal position as soon as possible, while it is dislocated, so that the arm swells or an abscess forms.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And during the return process, you should place the painful hand on a board and extend the other hand's hand, then align it so that its palm is placed in line with the appearance of the joint, and hold it until it heals.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	In all cases, you should check if it is properly in place;
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then have the patient place the back of their hand on a board during extension and retraction.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is in the back of the hand, then have the patient place the back of his hand on the table and you place your hand on the appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, it's indeed so.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, if the pressure of plaster salves on the abscesses and then lets it be without further recurrence.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, and you cannot put it back after some days, if the joint remains twisted;
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and does not harm him as long as his hands are swollen, and cannot constrain anything at all:
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	therefore know that the nerve is cut, or the artery;
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is no other means except to apply the cautery in the case, and by chance it is not worth any other thing.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the arms are in place, put on the plaster that we have described, then apply pressure and leave it for five days, then release and leave him like this.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he cannot move it well, and there is no swelling, with hot water, and rub it until it becomes clean.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	of the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Never let the shoulder joint of the hand be dislocated to each side, never on the back of the palm or belly;
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	Therefore lift the head, and hold the dislocated shoulder in your hands until it heals, then support the neck of the head, and guide it towards the part where it was separated.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and let it be for two days, and then place him evenly on that day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and bind him as we have said, and do the release of the day, and let him move, and rebind him at night;
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this often, until it is tight, and do so similarly, if it is dislocated in the chest of the hand, and do it like you have done before, until he heals;
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	and similarly do so when it is dislocated on the other side.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	Careful repositioning of the ankle, care of the back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When it's dislocated in the back or neck, or there are multiple dislocated (shoulders), if there is no treatment, for death comes to the patient quickly.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the signs are that the digestive actions jump without volition, nor can they be held, and many times soften any member, or both legs or both arms or one.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And many times the cheekbones move to four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	That which moves at the back is called 'Gilbositez':
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The treatment is that you should reward when Gilbositez comes from childhood:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	If there is no cure or healing at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from childbirth or impacts or similar matters, the old methods of treatment through great words say, they have no benefit in all great ways;
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	but I have abbreviated it according to my intention and formed tools in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that when Gilbositez comes down towards the groin, neither harm nor healing occurs;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also know that what comes directly to the two ribs, and one cannot cure outside of this precisely which goes to the back, as I say;
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And know that the body's tissues extend above its surface to one side in such a way that there is tension on it, so it does not get bruised;
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then stick the first thorn into the head in the earth forms, and the other at points, and tie a band around them under the armpits of the body tissue, and the other at hips, and knees, and ankles;
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	And two attendants know the bands, one at the head and the others at points, among the two thorns;
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	And be well closed, the thorn as we have said, and the patient puts her palms on the prick forms, until she regains consciousness.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not return through this treatment, take a board of three arms long, and place it over the wound. If the patient is on their side with the diseased limb towards the front, have someone hold onto one end of the board near the wound. Then put the middle part of the board under the spine;
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and place his elbows on the other end of the board, and press well, until he returns to his senses at his original position;
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you see that it turns around the elbow that bends towards the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And if you put two fire sticks at the elbow of the sick person's arm, one hand-length away from each other and towards his elbows. Leave an inch between each stick, directly above and below them.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	And place in each ember twigs or the turning bone, and make sure the embers are firmly in the ground, so they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	And in each pair of embers place one turning ember, so they cause the bone to turn, and include two small twigs about the length of a palm for turning the bone.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	And then tie the ligament that's among the muscles at the elbow towards the head, and the other ligament at the feet on the other elbow, and each of the assistants turns their elbow all along the ligament, and the masters place the spine evenly as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it's even, then place on plaster with abundant egg whites, and then the oil, and then the incense from a tablet of three inches long, which purges the inflamed area and the healthy part of the spine, then tie with a ligament as we have said, and treat the patient with subtle irritation until it's healthy.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	And if no healing comes at the end of health, then it is necessary to administer softening and soothing medicines, with the aid that we have mentioned earlier.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	And each time administer a piece of flax, and each time the appearance comes in the lower spine at the back, take care that it is a dislocation;
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	And it's the bone that opens, so we must not presume anything about it:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	By chance it would bring death.
des dislocations de la hainche	Dislocations of the hip
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Know that the joints of the hip and shoulder come only from dislocations, not like other joints.
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	And the hip joint is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	Beneath and removed, and forward and backward;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	And more beneath elsewhere, and somewhat dislocated in front and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of his dislocation beneath is that when one joins the diseased leg with the healthy one, it's longer, and the diseased knee opens more than the healthy one, and the diseased knee cannot bend back;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And it is the limbs that are swollen above with pus because the shoulder of the roast comes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him who comes to the death, is that this event is contrary to what precedes.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of him who experiences forward, is that his leg fits well according to its completion;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	Nevertheless, it does not bend the knee without pain, and if one wants to make him move, he cannot before, and holds his urine, and swells the groin, and when it goes, it passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs for him who approaches from behind, are that he cannot spread his foot out, nor double it, and one leg is more twisted than the other, and the ankle is softened, and there's swelling in the calf up to the knee over the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The restoration of this illusion of dislocation is that you return it when the dislocation is old, and it remains according to its position, if there is no treatment;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and there should be no assumption about it having healed.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And for those in which the dislocation is fresh, and there are four ways of dislocation, if you hurry to return the joint, and extend it both inside and out, and move it to the right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	By chance if it returns, and there is no need for any other treatment.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it doesn't return in this way, you should apply strong force and hold the leg firmly with both hands, or with one band where it is tied above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	And another attendant extends their hand over in such a way that they pinch his hands near his elbows, then drives them away with a single breath against the belly;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and some others grasp the nape of his neck;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	And extend up and down all at once, until the patient is lifted from the ground once, and remains hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This way of extension is common for four similar cases, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is indeed well.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not so, then it must take care according to its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is in the shoulder, you should remember to lift him up on his healthy side, then tie the bandage around the root of his elbow, and the part that's over the armpit. Then stretch the bandage towards the armpit, against resistance;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	Then request another attendant to hold his arms, and grasp the broad part of the patient's armpit, and extend it towards the front.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	it will return to its place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this way of dislocation is less severe than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot hold it in this way as we have said, then you should tie the two legs of the patient together tightly with a strong bandage around the two heels and the two knees, and so that the bad leg is extended by about two feet more than the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then hang it from the top of a pole, and above ground by two long lengths.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	Then instruct the attendant to hold the top of the armpit area, and have another attendant with the patient, who holds the armpit in place, because the joint is now returning quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is in front, if you lie the sick person down, just as we have said for someone with glibosity, and pull on the leg at the bad part of it precisely, and also on the knee.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two prongs, one on the head and another at the knee, then insert the prong between the thighs at the sick person's dislocation in the shape;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And place wet cloths around to prevent the patient from blistering, then extend each limb towards him, and have them set in an even position according to their hand at the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place it on 'ie' table and press it like we have said in the distension exercise, and let the patient lie on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, you must extend the bad leg quickly, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And place their palms so that they press against the painful part of the bad leg, then press with the other hand, and extend it downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is at the back, it does not require extending the patient downwards or lifting them from the ground. Instead, they should be positioned as if their buttocks were in the same place after being reset backwards, as we have explained regarding lying on the two buttocks;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	And if it is on their face, and the neck stretched as we said before, they must apply pressure to the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	And it will be right when the patient stretches their legs, and they will be equal in length;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Therefore adjust the hips, and apply the plaster, and bind with a bandage, so that the buttocks do not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And let them rest for three or four days, then release, and apply the plaster again;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	And if you see that they are equal, hold them as before, and let them be for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then release the dislocation, and treat him gently, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the shoulder joint dislocation
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knees are dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	This means, namely, internally and externally, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	And do not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs are that you command the patient to bend his leg at his knee. And if it does not adhere at his knee, know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all this is that you make the patient sit straight, and extend his leg if he can, and put your back on his buttocks, and place his foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take his shinbone between your palms, and pull it between your thumbs. Then bend both sides of the shinbone that form it.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And stretch out his leg with others assisting, until the knee returns to its place. And the signs are that he has correctly aligned his leg gently with his thigh;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	And place the plaster on, and have him lie with his leg straight at the knee, binding them together tightly for three or four days, then release.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And do not perform any surgery involving the joints until the limbs have been strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not present, apply strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it returns to its normal state.
de la dislocation dou talon	Of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are never completely dislocated and neither fully out of place, both inwards and outwards.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And you will know this by signs: that the ankle is swollen and tends forward to the part where it was dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The repositioning is gentle, and you should gently extend it to his hands when he is only slightly out of place.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is free from all pain completely, then you must make the patient lie straight and hold them up with the helpers by their leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then pull the leg towards you with your right hand, and then twice to your left, then stretch it upwards, and firmly position the leg upwards;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	And do this two times, as we have said, by holding and pulling the leg;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it returns, that is well;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If not, start the process again, because it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it cannot return like this, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and plant the post firmly in the earth between their buttocks, and wrap cloths around them, so that they do not bruise the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then the surgeons clean the wound, and other surgeons stretch out his legs or waist so they can be bound to the neck of the animal;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then extend each surgeon equally, and place the bundle so that it rests between the legs of the patient to hold the patient when they are extended.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then set the joints equal on his hands, and other surgeons cut the healthy leg at the knee, and the dislocated joint will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is to the point, place the plaster and bind it up, and apply pressure firmly, and then tie the leg to the animal, and guard the nerves that are above the ankle at the back, so the rope does not become too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if you apply pressure;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then release it on the third day or the fourth, and continue to guide the patient for three more days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if it goes beyond that time, it's not safe to say it won't dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if pus comes out at the incision site, it is necessary that you soothe it, just as we have said in other places, while it remains clean.
des dois	Of the cautery made with fire, command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulders are dislocated, if they can be properly stretched like in manual work, it's a simple task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in no corner of the back or foot, it's necessary that you make the patient lie on his full length or flat on a table completely straight, and place your foot where the joint opens. Then press with your foot firmly until he wakes up;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	And when he is straight, and there's nothing open, place a two-shouldered footrest under the sole of his foot, then press firmly, and let him rest three days, then release him.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And make them rest until they regain their senses.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	regarding injuries and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When injury accompanies dislocation, and one seeks to restore it, many times it has happened that the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you are not presumptuous in your treatment, and if you lack wisdom in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and slow, do not be hasty;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	And at the beginning of treatments aim to alleviate pain and pus, and let the patient be in God's hands, if you do not see hope for improvement;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you see hope, now reset the limb in its place, so that pus and life follow;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when the limb is in place, administer things that alleviate pus formation, and treat the wound as it should be, with drying ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is fracture with the dislocation, and small bones are broken, so treat them as we have instructed in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And protect yourself from entering the path of fear, as I have said, for it is according to your creator that you should live, and through knowledge arm yourself and protect your body.
